<h2>소스 코드 스니펫</h2>
<h3><code>161_lazycodex/README.md</code></h3>
<h2>🚀 Install</h2>
<p>One line. No global install, no <code>npm i -g</code>. Always use <code>bunx</code>:</p>
<pre><code class="language-bash">bunx lazycodex-ai install
</code></pre>
<p>This is shorthand for <code>bunx --package oh-my-openagent omo install --platform=codex</code>. For a fully autonomous, no-TUI setup:</p>
<pre><code class="language-bash">bunx lazycodex-ai install --no-tui --codex-autonomous
</code></pre>

<h3><code>000/03_overview_canonical_map.md</code></h3>
<h1>Overview Canonical Map</h1>
<p>This map resolves the apparent duplication between <code>/Users/jun/Developer/codex/000/</code> and <code>/Users/jun/Developer/codex/000_overview/</code> without deleting or moving files.</p>
<h2>Canonical Rule</h2>
<ul>
<li><code>/Users/jun/Developer/codex/000/</code> is the root overview index and short-entry reading spine.</li>
<li><code>/Users/jun/Developer/codex/000_overview/</code> is the deep overview source set.</li>
<li>If the same filename exists in both folders and content differs, keep both:
<ul>
<li>read <code>/Users/jun/Developer/codex/000/&#x3C;name></code> first for orientation,</li>
<li>read <code>/Users/jun/Developer/codex/000_overview/&#x3C;name></code> for detailed analysis.</li>
</ul>
</li>
<li>If content is identical, treat <code>/Users/jun/Developer/codex/000/&#x3C;name></code> as the navigation copy and <code>/Users/jun/Developer/codex/000_overview/&#x3C;name></code> as the deep-overview location until a later link audit decides whether deduplication is safe.</li>

<h3><code>000/03_overview_canonical_map.md</code></h3>
<h1>Overview Canonical Map</h1>
<p>This map resolves the apparent duplication between <code>/Users/jun/Developer/codex/000/</code> and <code>/Users/jun/Developer/codex/000_overview/</code> without deleting or moving files.</p>
<h2>Canonical Rule</h2>
<ul>
<li><code>/Users/jun/Developer/codex/000/</code> is the root overview index and short-entry reading spine.</li>
<li><code>/Users/jun/Developer/codex/000_overview/</code> is the deep overview source set.</li>
<li>If the same filename exists in both folders and content differs, keep both:
<ul>
<li>read <code>/Users/jun/Developer/codex/000/&#x3C;name></code> first for orientation,</li>
<li>read <code>/Users/jun/Developer/codex/000_overview/&#x3C;name></code> for detailed analysis.</li>
</ul>
</li>
<li>If content is identical, treat <code>/Users/jun/Developer/codex/000/&#x3C;name></code> as the navigation copy and <code>/Users/jun/Developer/codex/000_overview/&#x3C;name></code> as the deep-overview location until a later link audit decides whether deduplication is safe.</li>
</ul>

<h2>🚀 Install</h2>
<p>One line. No global install, no <code>npm i -g</code>. Always use <code>bunx</code>:</p>
<pre><code class="language-bash">bunx lazycodex-ai install
</code></pre>
<p>This is shorthand for <code>bunx --package oh-my-openagent omo install --platform=codex</code>. For a fully autonomous, no-TUI setup:</p>
<pre><code class="language-bash">bunx lazycodex-ai install --no-tui --codex-autonomous
</code></pre>

<h2>1. Identity — distribution layer, not agent runtime</h2>
<p>LazyCodex는 독립 코딩 에이전트가 아니다. README가 명시한다:</p>
<pre><code>// 161_lazycodex/README.md:79-81
LazyCodex is a thin distribution layer. The core engine is oh-my-openagent (OmO),
included as a submodule under `src/`.
</code></pre>
<table>
<thead>
<tr>
<th>Responsibility</th>
<th>Owner</th>
</tr>
</thead>
<tbody>
<tr>
<td>Terminal TUI, transcript rendering</td>
<td><strong>Codex</strong> (<code>121_openai-codex/codex-rs/tui</code>)</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>Model loop, tool dispatch, compaction</td>
<td><strong>Codex</strong></td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>OS sandbox, permission_mode, approvals</td>
<td><strong>Codex</strong></td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td><code>web_search</code>, <code>webfetch</code>, <code>spawn_agent</code></td>
<td><strong>Codex</strong></td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>npm install shorthand, marketplace snapshot</td>
<td><strong>LazyCodex</strong></td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>Hook subprocesses, LSP MCP, skills sync</td>
<td><strong>LC <code>plugins/omo</code></strong></td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>Ultrawork TOML roles, keyword directive</td>
<td><strong>LC <code>plugins/omo</code></strong></td>
</tr>
</tbody>
</table>
<p><code>.gitmodules</code>는 <code>src</code>를 <code>oh-my-openagent</code>로 선언하지만, Codex 플랫폼 경로의 <strong>실질 증거</strong>는 wrapper + <code>plugins/omo</code> 번들이다. OpenCode 전용 <code>ctx.client.tui.showToast</code> 같은 API는 submodule에 존재하나 <code>--platform=codex</code> install 시 활성화되지 않는다 (<code>01_lc_tui.md</code> §5).</p>

<h2>2. Distribution shim — <code>bin/lazycodex-ai.js</code></h2>
<p>전체 런타임은 28줄 Node forwarder다:</p>
<pre><code class="language-javascript">// 161_lazycodex/bin/lazycodex-ai.js:8-20
const commandArgs =
  forwardedArgs[0] === "install"
    ? ["--package", "oh-my-openagent", "omo", "install", "--platform=codex", ...forwardedArgs.slice(1)]
    : ["--package", "oh-my-openagent", "omo", ...forwardedArgs]

const result = spawnSync("bunx", commandArgs, {
  stdio: "inherit",
})
</code></pre>
<table>
<thead>
<tr>
<th>Line</th>
<th>Behavior</th>
</tr>
</thead>
<tbody>
<tr>
<td><code>:6-7</code></td>
<td><code>--dry-run</code> prints resolved argv without executing</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td><code>:9-11</code></td>
<td><code>install</code> injects <code>--platform=codex</code></td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td><code>:18-20</code></td>
<td><code>stdio: "inherit"</code> — child owns stdin/stdout (Codex/OmO TUI if any)</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td><code>:22-27</code></td>
<td>Propagates spawn error / exit status</td>
</tr>
</tbody>
</table>
<p>테스트가 계약을 고정한다: <code>161_lazycodex/test/lazycodex-ai-bin.test.mjs</code> — install vs non-install forwarding.</p>
<p><strong>Negative finding:</strong> <code>grep</code> of <code>161_lazycodex/bin/</code> shows no config parser, no TOML reader, no model router — only <code>spawnSync</code>.</p>

<h2>4. Axis synthesis — prompt &#x26; context (002)</h2>
<p>LazyCodex는 provider message JSON을 조립하지 않는다. Context는 Codex hook 이벤트로 주입된다.</p>
<pre><code class="language-json">// 161_lazycodex/plugins/omo/hooks/hooks.json — event map
"SessionStart": [ rules session-start, telemetry session-start ],
"UserPromptSubmit": [ rules, ultrawork-detector.py, ultragoal ],
"PostToolUse": [ comment-checker, lsp, rules (apply_patch) ],
"PostCompact": [ rules post-compact ]
</code></pre>
<p>Rules static injection pipeline (<code>components/rules/src/codex-hook.ts:212-247</code>):</p>
<ol>
<li>Read env config — skip if <code>disabled</code>, <code>mode === "off"</code>, or <code>mode === "dynamic"</code></li>
<li><code>engine.loadStaticRules(cwd)</code> discovers instruction files</li>
<li>Filter rules already in transcript (<code>:250-274</code>)</li>
<li>Emit JSON with <code>hookSpecificOutput.additionalContext</code> (<code>:455-462</code>)</li>
</ol>
<p>Ultrawork keyword trigger:</p>
<pre><code class="language-python"># 161_lazycodex/plugins/omo/components/ultrawork/hooks/ultrawork-detector.py:21-22
ULTRAWORK_PATTERN = re.compile(r"\b(?:ultrawork|ulw)\b", re.IGNORECASE)
</code></pre>
<p>Hook은 <strong>항상 exit 0</strong> — advisory injection, permission gate 아님.</p>

<p>LC-owned tool surface = <strong>LSP MCP stdio server</strong> 하나뿐:</p>
<pre><code class="language-json">// 161_lazycodex/plugins/omo/.mcp.json:1-8
{
  "mcpServers": {
    "lsp": {
      "command": "node",
      "args": ["./components/lsp/packages/lsp-tools-mcp/dist/cli.js", "mcp"],
      "cwd": "."
    }
  }
}
</code></pre>
<p>MCP handler (<code>components/lsp/packages/lsp-tools-mcp/src/mcp.ts:44-76</code>):</p>
<ul>
<li><code>initialize</code> → capabilities <code>{ tools: { listChanged: false } }</code></li>
<li><code>tools/list</code> → <code>lsp_diagnostics</code>, <code>lsp_rename</code>, <code>symbols</code>, etc.</li>
<li><code>tools/call</code> → language server subprocess with <code>shell: false</code></li>
</ul>
<p>PostToolUse hooks는 <strong>모델이 호출하는 tool이 아님</strong> — Codex lifecycle에서 subprocess로 실행:</p>
<table>
<thead>
<tr>
<th>Event</th>
<th>Matcher</th>
<th>Timeout</th>
</tr>
</thead>
<tbody>
<tr>
<td>PostToolUse</td>
<td><code>^(apply_patch|write|Write|edit|…)$</code></td>
<td>comment-checker 30s, lsp 60s</td>
</tr>
</tbody>
</table>
<p>Exa, Tavily, browser, filesystem MCP — <strong>snapshot에 없음</strong> (<code>aggregate.test.mjs:60-70</code>).</p>

<p><strong>Surfaces LC does NOT own:</strong> <code>codex-rs/app-server</code>, OpenCode server, IDE JSON-RPC daemons.</p>
<p><strong>Sandbox:</strong> LC configures hook subprocess timeouts and PostToolUse <code>decision: block</code> — not seatbelt/bwrap/seccomp. Codex <code>permission_mode</code> in hook stdin is read-only consumption.</p>
<p><strong>Config:</strong> No <code>.lazycodexrc</code>. Three layers: (1) zero-parser CLI shim, (2) frozen <code>.agents/plugins/marketplace.json</code>, (3) component env knobs (<code>CODEX_RULES_*</code>, <code>.codex/lsp-client.json</code>, <code>.omo/ultragoal/*.json</code>). Real <code>~/.codex/config.toml</code> mutations happen inside OmO installer.</p>

37:T63a2,<h2>기초 설명</h2>
<p>LazyCodex is a <strong>thin distribution wrapper</strong> over <a href="https://github.com/code-yeongyu/oh-my-openagent">oh-my-openagent (OmO)</a>. It does not ship Ratatui, Ink, blessed, or any terminal frame renderer. The user's interactive session is the <strong>Codex CLI TUI</strong>; LazyCodex contributes install/bootstrap plumbing, bundled Codex plugin hooks (with <code>statusMessage</code> strings during hook subprocesses), and documentation.</p>
<h2>이 문서에서 다루는 것</h2>
<ul>

<ol start="3">

</ol>

<li>
<ol start="4">

</ol>
</li>
<li>
<ol start="5">

<li>OpenCode install TUI (<code>@clack/prompts</code>)</li>

<ol start="6">
<li>What the user actually sees on Codex</li>
</ol>
</li>
<li>
<ol start="7">
<li>Negative evidence — grep bar</li>
</ol>
</li>
<li>
<ol start="8">
<li>Hook subprocess I/O model (not a terminal app)</li>
</ol>
</li>
<li>
<ol start="9">

<h2>코퍼스 — 001_tui-design/01_lc_tui.md (심화)</h2>
<h1>LazyCodex (<code>lc</code>) — TUI Design</h1>
<blockquote>
<p><strong>분석 스냅샷</strong>: <code>/Users/jun/Developer/codex/161_lazycodex/</code> (source checkout). <strong>런타임 TUI 없음</strong> — interactive rendering is entirely delegated to the Codex host (<code>121_openai-codex/codex-rs/tui</code>).</p>
</blockquote>
<p>LazyCodex is a <strong>thin distribution wrapper</strong> over <a href="https://github.com/code-yeongyu/oh-my-openagent">oh-my-openagent (OmO)</a>. It does not ship Ratatui, Ink, blessed, or any terminal frame renderer. The user's interactive session is the <strong>Codex CLI TUI</strong>; LazyCodex contributes install/bootstrap plumbing, bundled Codex plugin hooks (with <code>statusMessage</code> strings during hook subprocesses), and documentation.</p>
<h2>Architecture</h2>
<pre><code class="language-mermaid">flowchart TD
  User["User terminal"] --> LC["lazycodex-ai.js shim"]
  LC -->|"bunx --package oh-my-openagent omo install --platform=codex"| OMO["OmO installer"]
  OMO --> CX["Codex host TUI&#x3C;br/>(codex-rs/tui)"]
  CX --> Plugin["plugins/omo hooks"]
  Plugin -->|"statusMessage during hook"| CX
  LC -.->|"no renderer"| NR["❌ no LC-owned TUI loop"]
  OMO_OC["src/ OmO submodule&#x3C;br/>(OpenCode path only)"] -.->|"ctx.client.tui.showToast"| OC["OpenCode TUI"]
</code></pre>
<hr>
<h2>1. Distribution shim — no runtime TUI</h2>
<p>The npm binary is a synchronous <code>bunx</code> forwarder. It never opens alternate screen buffers, handles keyboard input, or draws widgets.</p>
<pre><code class="language-javascript">// 161_lazycodex/bin/lazycodex-ai.js:8-20
const commandArgs =
  forwardedArgs[0] === "install"
    ? ["--package", "oh-my-openagent", "omo", "install", "--platform=codex", ...forwardedArgs.slice(1)]
    : ["--package", "oh-my-openagent", "omo", ...forwardedArgs]

const result = spawnSync("bunx", commandArgs, {
  stdio: "inherit",
})
</code></pre>
<p><strong>Key behaviors:</strong></p>
<table>
<thead>
<tr>
<th>Line range</th>
<th>Behavior</th>
</tr>
</thead>
<tbody>
<tr>
<td><code>:6-7</code></td>
<td><code>--dry-run</code> prints the resolved <code>bunx</code> argv without executing</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td><code>:9-11</code></td>
<td><code>install</code> subcommand adds <code>--platform=codex</code> to OmO installer</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td><code>:18-20</code></td>
<td><code>stdio: "inherit"</code> — child owns stdin/stdout/stderr (Codex or OmO TUI if any)</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td><code>:22-27</code></td>
<td>Propagates spawn error / exit status; no LC error UI</td>
</tr>
</tbody>
</table>
<p>The README explicitly positions LazyCodex as a distribution layer, not a UI product:</p>
<pre><code>// 161_lazycodex/README.md:79-81
LazyCodex is a thin distribution layer. The core engine is oh-my-openagent (OmO),
included as a submodule under `src/`.
</code></pre>
<hr>
<h2>2. <code>--no-tui</code> is install-time only</h2>
<p>README documents a non-interactive install path:</p>
<pre><code class="language-bash"># 161_lazycodex/README.md:38-41
bunx lazycodex-ai install --no-tui --codex-autonomous
</code></pre>
<p>This flag applies to the <strong>OmO/Codex install wizard</strong>, not to suppressing Codex's runtime session TUI. After install, the user still interacts through Codex's native terminal UI when running an agent session.</p>
<p>Contrast: OmO's OpenCode installer uses <code>@clack/prompts</code> for a dedicated install TUI (<code>src/src/cli/tui-installer.ts</code>), which LazyCodex does not invoke on the Codex platform path.</p>
<hr>
<h2>3. Codex plugin hook status messages (host-rendered)</h2>
<p>While LazyCodex does not render frames, the bundled <code>plugins/omo</code> plugin registers <strong>status messages</strong> that Codex displays during hook subprocess execution:</p>
<pre><code class="language-json">// 161_lazycodex/plugins/omo/hooks/hooks.json:7-11
{
  "type": "command",
  "command": "node \"${PLUGIN_ROOT}/components/rules/dist/cli.js\" hook session-start",
  "timeout": 10,
  "statusMessage": "loading OMO project rules"
}
</code></pre>

<th>Timeout (s)</th>
</tr>
</thead>
<tbody>
<tr>

<td>10</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td><code>SessionStart</code> → telemetry</td>
<td><em>(none)</em></td>
<td>5</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td><code>UserPromptSubmit</code> → rules</td>

<td>10</td>
</tr>

<td><code>checking OMO ultragoal steering</code></td>
<td>10</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td><code>PostToolUse</code> → comment-checker</td>

<td>30</td>
</tr>

<td>60</td>
</tr>

<p>These strings are <strong>host chrome</strong>, not LC-owned widgets. Codex decides placement, duration, and styling.</p>
<hr>
<h2>4. Plugin manifest — interface metadata only</h2>
<pre><code class="language-json">// 161_lazycodex/plugins/omo/.codex-plugin/plugin.json:17-34
"interface": {
  "displayName": "OMO",
  "shortDescription": "Unified local Codex components",
  "longDescription": "OMO exposes the local Codex Rules, Comment Checker, LSP, Ultrawork, and Ultragoal components as one plugin namespace...",
  "capabilities": ["Hooks", "MCP Tools", "Code Intelligence", "Workflow", "Context Injection"],
  "defaultPrompt": [
    "Use OMO LSP diagnostics on this workspace.",
    "Show which OMO rules matched this file.",
    "ulw: run this change with evidence."
  ],
  "brandColor": "#7C3AED"
}
</code></pre>
<p>The <code>interface</code> block is marketplace/catalog metadata for Codex plugin discovery — not a TUI theme or layout definition.</p>
<hr>
<h2>5. OmO submodule — OpenCode TUI path (reference only)</h2>
<p>LazyCodex vendors OmO under <code>161_lazycodex/src/</code> (git submodule). On <strong>OpenCode</strong>, OmO hooks call host TUI APIs. This path is <strong>not</strong> active when <code>--platform=codex</code> is used, but documents the delegation pattern LC inherits upstream:</p>
<pre><code class="language-typescript">// 161_lazycodex/src/src/plugin/hooks/create-session-hooks.ts:165-175
toast: async ({ title, message, variant, duration }) => {
  await ctx.client.tui
    .showToast({
      body: {
        title,
        message,
        variant: variant ?? "warning",
        duration: duration ?? 5000,
      },
    })
    .catch(() => {})
},
</code></pre>
<p>Model-fallback and auto-update hooks use the same <code>ctx.client.tui.showToast</code> channel (<code>:187-195</code>). LazyCodex on Codex <strong>does not</strong> expose <code>ctx.client.tui</code> — that API belongs to OpenCode's client SDK.</p>
<h3>OpenCode install TUI (<code>@clack/prompts</code>)</h3>
<pre><code class="language-typescript">// 161_lazycodex/src/src/cli/tui-installer.ts:16-20
export async function runTuiInstaller(args: InstallArgs, version: string): Promise&#x3C;number> {
  if (!process.stdin.isTTY || !process.stdout.isTTY) {
    console.error("Error: Interactive installer requires a TTY. Use --non-interactive or set environment variables directly.")
    return 1
  }
</code></pre>
<p>OpenCode installer: spinners, intro/outro banners, config prompts. Codex install via <code>lazycodex-ai install</code> delegates to OmO's Codex-specific installer (no <code>@clack</code> in the LC shim itself).</p>

<hr>
<h2>8. Hook subprocess I/O model (not a terminal app)</h2>
<p>Rules hook emits JSON on stdout for Codex to parse:</p>
<pre><code class="language-typescript">// 161_lazycodex/plugins/omo/components/rules/src/codex-hook.ts:455-462
function formatAdditionalContextOutput(eventName: ContextInjectionHookEventName, additionalContext: string): string {
  if (additionalContext.trim().length === 0) return "";
  return `${JSON.stringify({
    hookSpecificOutput: {
      hookEventName: eventName,
      additionalContext,
    },
  })}\n`;
}
</code></pre>
<p>Ultrawork detector writes plain-text directive to stdout (Codex treats non-JSON stdout as <code>additional_context</code>):</p>
<pre><code class="language-python"># 161_lazycodex/plugins/omo/components/ultrawork/hooks/ultrawork-detector.py:285-290
def main() -> None:
    payload = _load_payload()
    if payload is not None and _should_inject(payload):
        _ = sys.stdout.write(ULTRAWORK_DIRECTIVE)
        _ = sys.stdout.flush()
    sys.exit(0)
</code></pre>
<p>No curses/ANSI layout — only structured hook output consumed by the host TUI layer.</p>
<hr>

{

<h2>10. Test contract — hooks stay component-isolated</h2>
<pre><code class="language-javascript">// 161_lazycodex/plugins/omo/test/aggregate.test.mjs:38-57
test("#given isolated components #when hooks are inspected #then commands stay inside component roots", async () => {
  const hooks = await readJson("hooks/hooks.json");
  const text = JSON.stringify(hooks);
  const componentMarkers = [
    "components/comment-checker/dist/cli.js",
    "components/lsp/dist/cli.js",
    "components/rules/dist/cli.js",
    // ...
  ];
  for (const marker of componentMarkers) {
    assert.match(text, new RegExp(marker.replaceAll("/", "\\/")));
  }
});
</code></pre>
<p>Aggregate tests verify hook command paths — subprocess invocation, not UI rendering.</p>

<hr>
<h2>12. Design boundary</h2>
<p>LazyCodex <strong>never</strong> draws frames, manages cursor state, or handles keyboard input. Any perceived "TUI feature" is either:</p>
<ol>
<li><strong>Codex host</strong> — chat loop, tool rendering, approvals, compaction UI</li>
<li><strong>Hook side-effects</strong> — <code>statusMessage</code> during subprocess hooks</li>
<li><strong>OmO OpenCode</strong> (upstream submodule) — <code>showToast</code>, install wizard — not on Codex platform path</li>
</ol>
<p>Do not document LC as having a TUI crate or render loop. Cross-reference <code>01_co_tui.md</code> for interactive depth.</p>
<hr>
<h2>13. Operational workflow (user perspective)</h2>
<ol>
<li>User runs <code>bunx lazycodex-ai install</code> (or <code>install --no-tui --codex-autonomous</code>)</li>
<li>OmO installs Codex plugin marketplace entry + <code>omo</code> plugin under <code>~/.codex/</code></li>
<li>User starts <strong><code>codex</code></strong> (or IDE integration) — Codex TUI renders the session</li>
<li>On session start, OMO rules hook runs; user may briefly see <code>loading OMO project rules</code></li>
<li>User types prompt; optional <code>ulw</code>/<code>ultrawork</code> triggers ultrawork directive injection</li>
<li>All subsequent UI — tool cards, diffs, MCP panels — is Codex-native</li>
</ol>
<hr>

<table>

</tr>

</tr>

</tr>
</tbody>
</table>
<p>LC shim does not retry failed installs or present interactive error menus.</p>

38:T7799,<h2>기초 설명</h2>
<p>LazyCodex does not assemble provider messages, call models directly, or implement compaction. Its prompt/context surface is the bundled <code>plugins/omo</code> Codex plugin: lifecycle hooks that emit <code>hookSpecificOutput.additionalContext</code>, keyword-triggered ultrawork directives, ultragoal steering, lazy-loaded skills, and LSP MCP tool context when invoked.</p>
<h2>이 문서에서 다루는 것</h2>
<ul>
<li>Architecture</li>
<li>
<ol>
<li>Distribution boundary — no LC-owned system prompt</li>
</ol>
</li>
<li>
<ol start="2">
<li>Hook registry — context injection events</li>
</ol>
</li>
<li>
<ol start="3">
<li>Rules component — static context injection</li>
</ol>
</li>
<li>SessionStart / UserPromptSubmit</li>
<li>Transcript deduplication</li>
<li>PostToolUse — dynamic context</li>
<li>PostCompact — cache reset</li>
<li>
<ol start="4">
<li>Ultrawork keyword directive</li>
</ol>
</li>
<li>
<ol start="5">
<li>Ultragoal steering</li>
</ol>
</li>
<li>
<ol start="6">
<li>Post-edit context — block decisions with additionalContext</li>
</ol>
</li>
<li>Comment checker</li>
</ul>
<h2>소스 코드 스니펫</h2>
<h3>README / docs</h3>
<pre><code class="language-mermaid">flowchart TD
  User["User prompt"] --> CX["Codex host prompt assembly"]
  CX --> H1["SessionStart hooks"]
  CX --> H2["UserPromptSubmit hooks"]
  CX --> H3["PostToolUse hooks"]
  CX --> H4["PostCompact hooks"]
  H1 --> Rules["rules: static context"]
  H2 --> Rules
  H2 --> ULW["ultrawork-detector.py"]
  H2 --> UG["ultragoal steering"]
  H3 --> RulesD["rules: dynamic context"]
  H3 --> CC["comment-checker block"]
  H3 --> LSP["LSP diagnostics block"]
  H4 --> RulesR["rules: cache reset"]
  Rules --> AC["additionalContext JSON"]
  ULW --> AC2["plain-text directive"]
  UG --> AC
  Skills["skills/ SKILL.md"] -.->|"lazy load on invoke"| CX
  MCP["LSP MCP tools"] -.->|"tool turn context"| CX
</code></pre>
<h3>README / docs</h3>
<pre><code class="language-javascript">// 161_lazycodex/bin/lazycodex-ai.js:8-11
const commandArgs =
  forwardedArgs[0] === "install"

<h3>README / docs</h3>
<pre><code class="language-typescript">// 161_lazycodex/plugins/omo/components/rules/src/codex-hook.ts:276-287
function isRuleAlreadyInTranscript(rule: LoadedRule, transcriptText: string): boolean {
  const bodyNeedle = rule.body.trim().slice(0, 2_000);
  if (bodyNeedle.length === 0 || !transcriptText.includes(bodyNeedle)) {
    return false;
  }
  const markers = [
    `Instructions from: ${rule.path}`,
    `Instructions from: ${rule.realPath}`,
    rule.relativePath.length === 0 ? null : rule.relativePath,
  ].filter((marker): marker is string => marker !== null);
  return markers.some((marker) => transcriptText.includes(marker));
}
</code></pre>

    return "";

}

def _should_inject(payload: dict[str, object]) -> bool:

<h3>README / docs</h3>

export async function applyUserPromptUltragoalSteering(payload: UserPromptSubmitPayload): Promise&#x3C;string> {
  if (payload.hook_event_name !== "UserPromptSubmit") return "";
  const proposal = parseUltragoalSteeringDirective(payload.prompt);
  if (proposal === null) return "";
  const result = await steerUltragoal(payload.cwd, proposal);
  if (!result.accepted) return "";
  return JSON.stringify({
    status: "accepted",
    kind: result.audit.kind,
    source: result.audit.source,
    deduped: result.deduped,
  });
}
</code></pre>

<h2>코퍼스 — 002_prompt-context/02_lc_prompt.md (심화)</h2>
<h1>LazyCodex — Prompt / Context Assembly</h1>
<blockquote>
<p><strong>분석 스냅샷</strong>: <code>/Users/jun/Developer/codex/161_lazycodex/</code> + OmO <code>src/</code> submodule — <strong>no local LLM loop</strong>; context is injected via Codex plugin hooks into the host-managed prompt.</p>
</blockquote>
<p>LazyCodex does not assemble provider messages, call models directly, or implement compaction. Its prompt/context surface is the bundled <code>plugins/omo</code> Codex plugin: lifecycle hooks that emit <code>hookSpecificOutput.additionalContext</code>, keyword-triggered ultrawork directives, ultragoal steering, lazy-loaded skills, and LSP MCP tool context when invoked.</p>
<h2>Architecture</h2>
<pre><code class="language-mermaid">flowchart TD
  User["User prompt"] --> CX["Codex host prompt assembly"]
  CX --> H1["SessionStart hooks"]
  CX --> H2["UserPromptSubmit hooks"]
  CX --> H3["PostToolUse hooks"]
  CX --> H4["PostCompact hooks"]
  H1 --> Rules["rules: static context"]
  H2 --> Rules
  H2 --> ULW["ultrawork-detector.py"]
  H2 --> UG["ultragoal steering"]
  H3 --> RulesD["rules: dynamic context"]
  H3 --> CC["comment-checker block"]
  H3 --> LSP["LSP diagnostics block"]
  H4 --> RulesR["rules: cache reset"]
  Rules --> AC["additionalContext JSON"]
  ULW --> AC2["plain-text directive"]
  UG --> AC
  Skills["skills/ SKILL.md"] -.->|"lazy load on invoke"| CX
  MCP["LSP MCP tools"] -.->|"tool turn context"| CX
</code></pre>
<hr>
<h2>1. Distribution boundary — no LC-owned system prompt</h2>
<pre><code class="language-javascript">// 161_lazycodex/bin/lazycodex-ai.js:8-11
const commandArgs =
  forwardedArgs[0] === "install"
    ? ["--package", "oh-my-openagent", "omo", "install", "--platform=codex", ...forwardedArgs.slice(1)]
    : ["--package", "oh-my-openagent", "omo", ...forwardedArgs]
</code></pre>
<p>The npm package forwards to OmO; it never reads <code>AGENTS.md</code>, never tokenizes, never merges chat history. All prompt assembly is <strong>Codex host + plugin hooks</strong>.</p>
<p>Plugin manifest declares context capabilities:</p>
<pre><code class="language-json">// 161_lazycodex/plugins/omo/.codex-plugin/plugin.json:14-16,23
"skills": "./skills/",
"hooks": "./hooks/hooks.json",
"mcpServers": "./.mcp.json",
"capabilities": ["Hooks", "MCP Tools", "Code Intelligence", "Workflow", "Context Injection"]
</code></pre>
<hr>
<h2>2. Hook registry — context injection events</h2>
<pre><code class="language-json">// 161_lazycodex/plugins/omo/hooks/hooks.json:3-97
"SessionStart": [ rules session-start, telemetry session-start ],
"UserPromptSubmit": [ rules user-prompt-submit, ultrawork-detector.py, ultragoal user-prompt-submit ],
"PostToolUse": [ comment-checker + lsp (edit matchers), rules post-tool-use (apply_patch) ],
"PostCompact": [ rules post-compact (manual|auto) ]
</code></pre>
<table>
<thead>
<tr>
<th>Event</th>
<th>Components</th>
<th>Context type</th>
</tr>
</thead>
<tbody>
<tr>
<td><code>SessionStart</code></td>
<td>rules, telemetry</td>
<td>Static rules → <code>additionalContext</code></td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td><code>UserPromptSubmit</code></td>
<td>rules, ultrawork, ultragoal</td>
<td>Static rules + keyword directive + goal steering</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td><code>PostToolUse</code></td>
<td>comment-checker, lsp, rules</td>
<td>Block decisions + dynamic rules</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td><code>PostCompact</code></td>
<td>rules</td>
<td>Session cache reset (no context emit)</td>
</tr>
</tbody>
</table>
<p>Telemetry hook on <code>SessionStart</code> tracks activity (PostHog) — not prompt text (<code>hooks.json:14-22</code>).</p>
<hr>
<h2>3. Rules component — static context injection</h2>
<h3>SessionStart / UserPromptSubmit</h3>
<pre><code class="language-typescript">// 161_lazycodex/plugins/omo/components/rules/src/codex-hook.ts:82-102
export async function runSessionStartHook(
  input: CodexSessionStartInput,
  options: CodexRulesHookOptions = {},
): Promise&#x3C;string> {
  const cachePath = sessionCachePath(input.session_id, options.pluginDataRoot);
  if (input.source === "clear") {
    clearSessionState(cachePath);
  } else if (input.source !== "resume" &#x26;&#x26; !hasPostCompactPending(cachePath)) {
    clearSessionState(cachePath);
  }
  // ...
  return runStaticInjection(input.cwd, transcriptPath, "SessionStart", cachePath, options, ...);
}
</code></pre>
<p>Static injection pipeline (<code>:212-247</code>):</p>
<ol>
<li>Read config from environment — skip if <code>disabled</code>, <code>mode === "off"</code>, or <code>mode === "dynamic"</code> (<code>:220-223</code>)</li>
<li><code>engine.loadStaticRules(cwd)</code> discovers project/user/bundled instruction files</li>
<li>Filter rules already present in transcript (<code>filterRulesAlreadyInTranscript</code>, <code>:250-274</code>)</li>
<li>Format block via <code>engine.formatStatic(rules)</code> (<code>:242</code>)</li>
<li>Mark injected rules in session cache to prevent duplicates</li>
<li>Emit JSON:</li>
</ol>
<pre><code class="language-typescript">// 161_lazycodex/plugins/omo/components/rules/src/codex-hook.ts:455-462
return `${JSON.stringify({
  hookSpecificOutput: {
    hookEventName: eventName,
    additionalContext,
  },
})}\n`;
</code></pre>
<h3>Transcript deduplication</h3>
<p>Rules avoid re-injecting content already in the session transcript:</p>
<pre><code class="language-typescript">// 161_lazycodex/plugins/omo/components/rules/src/codex-hook.ts:276-287
function isRuleAlreadyInTranscript(rule: LoadedRule, transcriptText: string): boolean {
  const bodyNeedle = rule.body.trim().slice(0, 2_000);
  if (bodyNeedle.length === 0 || !transcriptText.includes(bodyNeedle)) {
    return false;
  }
  const markers = [
    `Instructions from: ${rule.path}`,
    `Instructions from: ${rule.realPath}`,
    rule.relativePath.length === 0 ? null : rule.relativePath,
  ].filter((marker): marker is string => marker !== null);
  return markers.some((marker) => transcriptText.includes(marker));
}
</code></pre>
<p>Transcript parsing also extracts JSON-line string values for nested content search (<code>:299-314</code>).</p>
<h3>PostToolUse — dynamic context</h3>
<p>After edit-like tools, rules inject <strong>file-targeted</strong> dynamic context:</p>
<pre><code class="language-typescript">// 161_lazycodex/plugins/omo/components/rules/src/codex-hook.ts:129-139
export async function runPostToolUseHook(...) {
  const config = configFromEnvironment(options.env);
  if (config.disabled || config.mode === "off" || config.mode === "static") {
    return "";
  }
  const targetPaths = extractCodexToolPaths(input, input.cwd);
  // fingerprint changed files → loadDynamicRules → formatDynamic
}
</code></pre>
<p>Dynamic mode skips static-only configs; static mode skips dynamic post-edit injection — modes are mutually exclusive at runtime.</p>
<h3>PostCompact — cache reset</h3>
<pre><code class="language-typescript">// 161_lazycodex/plugins/omo/components/rules/src/codex-hook.ts:104-110
export async function runPostCompactHook(...) {
  markSessionCompacted(sessionCachePath(input.session_id, options.pluginDataRoot));
  return "";
}
</code></pre>
<p>After compaction, pending re-injection channels are flagged so static rules can re-apply on next prompt (<code>isPostCompactPending</code>, used at <code>:117</code>, <code>:154</code>).</p>
<hr>
<h2>4. Ultrawork keyword directive</h2>
<p>Python hook on <code>UserPromptSubmit</code> — word-bounded keyword match:</p>
<pre><code class="language-python"># 161_lazycodex/plugins/omo/components/ultrawork/hooks/ultrawork-detector.py:21-22
ULTRAWORK_PATTERN = re.compile(r"\b(?:ultrawork|ulw)\b", re.IGNORECASE)
</code></pre>
<p>Contract documented in module docstring (<code>:4-10</code>):</p>
<ul>
<li><strong>stdin</strong>: JSON with <code>prompt</code>, <code>hook_event_name</code>, session fields</li>
<li><strong>stdout</strong>: Full <code>ULTRAWORK_DIRECTIVE</code> text when matched; empty otherwise</li>
<li><strong>exit</strong>: Always <code>0</code> — never blocks the turn (<code>:10</code>, <code>:290</code>)</li>
</ul>
<p>Injection gate:</p>
<pre><code class="language-python"># 161_lazycodex/plugins/omo/components/ultrawork/hooks/ultrawork-detector.py:276-282
def _should_inject(payload: dict[str, object]) -> bool:
    if payload.get("hook_event_name") != "UserPromptSubmit":
        return False
    prompt = payload.get("prompt")
    if not isinstance(prompt, str) or not prompt:
        return False
    return ULTRAWORK_PATTERN.search(prompt) is not None
</code></pre>
<p>The directive (<code>ULTRAWORK_DIRECTIVE</code>, <code>:25-256</code>) is a large structured block covering:</p>
<ul>
<li>Mandatory first-line banner: <code>ULTRAWORK MODE ENABLED!</code></li>
<li>Role/goal constraints (evidence-driven, test-first + manual QA channels)</li>
<li>Manual-QA channels: HTTP, tmux, browser use, computer use</li>
<li>Bootstrap requirements: goal creation, parallel subagents, reviewer gate</li>
<li>Stop/retry rules</li>
</ul>
<p>Codex treats non-JSON stdout as raw <code>additional_context</code> — no <code>hookSpecificOutput</code> wrapper for this hook.</p>
<hr>
<h2>5. Ultragoal steering</h2>
<pre><code class="language-typescript">// 161_lazycodex/plugins/omo/components/ultragoal/src/codex-hook.ts:25-37
export async function applyUserPromptUltragoalSteering(payload: UserPromptSubmitPayload): Promise&#x3C;string> {
  if (payload.hook_event_name !== "UserPromptSubmit") return "";
  const proposal = parseUltragoalSteeringDirective(payload.prompt);
  if (proposal === null) return "";
  const result = await steerUltragoal(payload.cwd, proposal);
  if (!result.accepted) return "";
  return JSON.stringify({
    status: "accepted",
    kind: result.audit.kind,
    source: result.audit.source,
    deduped: result.deduped,
  });
}
</code></pre>
<p>Ultragoal mutates durable <code>.omo/ultragoal</code> plan/ledger state in the workspace when steering directives are accepted. Hook registered at <code>hooks.json:44-52</code> with <code>statusMessage: "checking OMO ultragoal steering"</code>.</p>
<p>Unlike ultrawork, ultragoal output is structured JSON status — not a large prompt block — but accepted steering affects subsequent turns via persisted goal files.</p>
<hr>
<h2>6. Post-edit context — block decisions with additionalContext</h2>
<h3>Comment checker</h3>
<pre><code class="language-typescript">// 161_lazycodex/plugins/omo/components/comment-checker/src/codex-hook.ts:60-65
return JSON.stringify({
  decision: "block",
  reason: formatWarnings(warnings),
});
</code></pre>
<p>Runs on mutation tools matched in <code>hooks.json:57</code> — injects block reason when AI-slop comments detected.</p>
<h3>LSP diagnostics</h3>
<pre><code class="language-typescript">// 161_lazycodex/plugins/omo/components/lsp/src/codex-hook.ts:55-63
const output: PostToolUseHookOutput = {
  decision: "block",
  reason,
  hookSpecificOutput: {
    hookEventName: "PostToolUse",
    additionalContext: reason,
  },
};
</code></pre>
<p>Blocks turn when LSP reports errors after edits (<code>MUTATION_TOOL_NAMES</code>, <code>:27</code>; <code>executeLspDiagnostics</code> with <code>severity: "error"</code>, <code>:31-33</code>).</p>
<p>These are <strong>prompt-adjacent</strong> — they can halt the tool loop and surface diagnostic text as context for the model's next turn.</p>
<hr>

<p>Skills are exposed via manifest <code>"skills": "./skills/"</code> — Codex lazy-loads <code>SKILL.md</code> bodies when the model or user invokes a skill; they are <strong>not</strong> prepended to every system prompt.</p>
<h3>Codex compatibility rewrite</h3>
<p>OpenCode-only orchestration examples get a compatibility preamble:</p>
<pre><code class="language-javascript">// 161_lazycodex/plugins/omo/scripts/sync-skills.mjs:16-30

<h2>8. LSP MCP — tool context (not base prompt)</h2>

<p>LSP tools (<code>diagnostics</code>, <code>goto_definition</code>, <code>rename</code>, etc.) contribute context <strong>when the model invokes them</strong> — not at session start. See <code>003_tool-runtime/03_lc_tool.md</code>.</p>

<h2>10. What LazyCodex does NOT implement</h2>
<table>
<thead>
<tr>
<th>Feature</th>
<th>Owner</th>
</tr>
</thead>
<tbody>
<tr>
<td>System prompt template</td>
<td>Codex host</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>Message list / roles</td>
<td>Codex host</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>Compaction algorithm</td>
<td>Codex host (<code>PostCompact</code> hook notifies rules only)</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>Token counting</td>
<td>Codex host</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>Model API request shape</td>
<td>Codex host</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>Provider routing</td>
<td>Codex host (+ OmO upstream for OpenCode)</td>
</tr>
</tbody>
</table>
<p>OmO submodule (<code>161_lazycodex/src/</code>) contains OpenCode-specific transforms (<code>messages-transform.ts</code>, <code>system-transform.ts</code>, <code>session-compacting.ts</code>) — <strong>not exercised</strong> on Codex platform install path.</p>

<hr>
<h2>12. Security / privacy notes</h2>
<ul>
<li><strong>Rules content</strong>: Arbitrary project instruction files merged into model context — trust model boundary</li>
<li><strong>Ultrawork directive</strong>: Large injected block changes agent behavior significantly — keyword-gated only</li>
<li><strong>Telemetry</strong>: PostHog on SessionStart — not prompt text (<code>components/telemetry/</code>)</li>
<li><strong>Transcript reads</strong>: Rules hook reads transcript JSONL for dedup — local filesystem only</li>
</ul>
<hr>
<h2>13. Test coverage</h2>
<pre><code class="language-javascript">// 161_lazycodex/plugins/omo/test/aggregate.test.mjs:22-36
assert.equal(manifest.name, "omo");
assert.equal(hookPath, "./hooks/hooks.json");
assert.equal(skillsPath, "./skills/");
</code></pre>
<p><code>sync-skills.test.mjs</code> verifies aggregate skill inventory and Codex compatibility block injection.</p>
<hr>
<h2>14. Operational workflow</h2>
<ol>
<li>Session starts → rules static context injected (project AGENTS-style files)</li>
<li>User submits prompt → rules re-evaluated; if <code>ulw</code> present, ultrawork directive appended</li>
<li>Ultragoal steering parsed; may update <code>.omo/ultragoal</code> ledger</li>
<li>Model acts with merged host + hook context</li>
<li>After edits → LSP/comment-checker may block; rules may inject file-specific dynamic context</li>
<li>On compaction → rules cache reset; static rules re-inject on next turn</li>
</ol>
<hr>
<h2>15. Evidence quality bar</h2>
<ul class="contains-task-list">
<li class="task-list-item"><input type="checkbox" checked disabled> Rules hook static/dynamic/compact paths with line numbers</li>
<li class="task-list-item"><input type="checkbox" checked disabled> Ultrawork detector contract and keyword pattern</li>

39:T6961,<h2>기초 설명</h2>
<p>LazyCodex has no LLM tool loop, permission engine, or sandbox. Runtime layers: (1) <code>lazycodex-ai.js</code> CLI forwarder, (2) Codex plugin hook commands, (3) LSP MCP JSON-RPC over stdio. Tool dispatch, streaming, and approval UX remain Codex-owned.</p>

const SERVER_NAME = "lsp";
const SERVER_VERSION = "0.1.0";
const DEFAULT_IDLE_TIMEOUT_MS = 10 * 60_000;

export async function handleLspMcpRequest(input: unknown): Promise&#x3C;JsonRpcResponse | undefined> {
  // ...
  if (method === "initialize") {
    return successResponse(id, {
      capabilities: { tools: { listChanged: false } },
      serverInfo: { name: SERVER_NAME, version: SERVER_VERSION },
      protocolVersion,
    });
  }
  if (method === "tools/list") {
    return successResponse(id, { tools: LSP_MCP_TOOLS.map(describeTool) });
  }
  if (method === "tools/call") {
    return handleToolCall(id, input["params"]);
  }
}

<h2>코퍼스 — 003_tool-runtime/03_lc_tool.md (심화)</h2>
<h1>LazyCodex — Tool Runtime</h1>
<blockquote>
<p><strong>분석 스냅샷</strong>: <code>/Users/jun/Developer/codex/161_lazycodex/</code> — <strong>no standalone tool dispatcher</strong>; Codex host executes tools; LC packages hook subprocesses and one LSP MCP stdio server.</p>
</blockquote>
<p>LazyCodex has no LLM tool loop, permission engine, or sandbox. Runtime layers: (1) <code>lazycodex-ai.js</code> CLI forwarder, (2) Codex plugin hook commands, (3) LSP MCP JSON-RPC over stdio. Tool dispatch, streaming, and approval UX remain Codex-owned.</p>
<h2>Architecture</h2>
<pre><code class="language-mermaid">flowchart TD
  Model["Codex model turn"] --> Host["Codex tool runtime"]
  Host --> Builtin["Host builtins&#x3C;br/>(bash, apply_patch, spawn_agent, …)"]
  Host --> MCP["MCP client"]
  MCP --> LSP["lsp MCP stdio server"]
  Host --> Hooks["PostToolUse hooks"]
  Hooks --> CC["comment-checker"]
  Hooks --> LSPH["lsp diagnostics hook"]
  Hooks --> Rules["rules dynamic"]
  LSP --> Tools["lsp_diagnostics, lsp_rename, …"]
  LSP --> LSProc["Language server subprocess"]
  Shim["lazycodex-ai.js"] -.->|"install only"| Host
</code></pre>
<hr>
<h2>1. CLI layer — not a tool runtime</h2>
<pre><code class="language-javascript">// 161_lazycodex/bin/lazycodex-ai.js:18-20
const result = spawnSync("bunx", commandArgs, {
  stdio: "inherit",
})
</code></pre>
<p>The npm bin forwards argv to <code>oh-my-openagent</code> via <code>bunx</code>. No tool registry, no JSON-RPC server, no model API. Install path adds <code>--platform=codex</code> (<code>:9-10</code>).</p>
<hr>
<h2>2. Plugin workspace — component isolation</h2>
<pre><code class="language-json">// 161_lazycodex/plugins/omo/package.json:8-21
"workspaces": [
  "components/comment-checker",
  "components/rules",
  "components/lsp",
  "components/lsp/packages/lsp-tools-mcp",
  "components/telemetry",
  "components/ultragoal",
  "components/ultrawork"
],
"scripts": {
  "build": "node scripts/sync-skills.mjs &#x26;&#x26; node ../scripts/sync-telemetry-component.mjs &#x26;&#x26; npm run build --workspaces --if-present",
  "test": "node --test test/*.test.mjs"
}
</code></pre>
<p>Each component builds a <code>dist/cli.js</code> hook entrypoint. Aggregate tests enforce hook commands reference <code>components/*/dist/</code> paths, not external npm package names (<code>aggregate.test.mjs:54-57</code>).</p>
<hr>

<p>PostToolUse matcher for quality hooks:</p>
<pre><code class="language-json">// 161_lazycodex/plugins/omo/hooks/hooks.json:57
"matcher": "^(apply_patch|write|Write|edit|Edit|multi_edit|multiedit|MultiEdit)$"
</code></pre>
<p>Hooks are <strong>not tools the model calls</strong> — Codex invokes them on lifecycle events. They can return <code>decision: "block"</code> to interrupt the tool loop.</p>
<hr>
<h2>4. LSP MCP server — the only LC-registered MCP</h2>
<pre><code class="language-json">// 161_lazycodex/plugins/omo/.mcp.json:1-9
{
  "mcpServers": {
    "lsp": {
      "command": "node",
      "args": ["./components/lsp/packages/lsp-tools-mcp/dist/cli.js", "mcp"],
      "cwd": "."
    }
  }
}
</code></pre>
<p>Aggregate test locks this contract:</p>
<pre><code class="language-javascript">// 161_lazycodex/plugins/omo/test/aggregate.test.mjs:60-70
assert.equal(server.command, "node");
assert.deepEqual(server.args, ["./components/lsp/packages/lsp-tools-mcp/dist/cli.js", "mcp"]);
assert.equal(server.cwd, ".");
</code></pre>
<p><strong>No</strong> Exa, Tavily, browser, or filesystem MCP servers in LC snapshot — LSP only.</p>
<hr>
<h2>5. MCP JSON-RPC implementation</h2>
<pre><code class="language-typescript">// 161_lazycodex/plugins/omo/components/lsp/packages/lsp-tools-mcp/src/mcp.ts:44-76
const SERVER_NAME = "lsp";
const SERVER_VERSION = "0.1.0";
const DEFAULT_IDLE_TIMEOUT_MS = 10 * 60_000;

export async function handleLspMcpRequest(input: unknown): Promise&#x3C;JsonRpcResponse | undefined> {
  // ...
  if (method === "initialize") {
    return successResponse(id, {
      capabilities: { tools: { listChanged: false } },
      serverInfo: { name: SERVER_NAME, version: SERVER_VERSION },
      protocolVersion,
    });
  }
  if (method === "tools/list") {
    return successResponse(id, { tools: LSP_MCP_TOOLS.map(describeTool) });
  }
  if (method === "tools/call") {
    return handleToolCall(id, input["params"]);
  }
}
</code></pre>
<p>Stdio server loop with idle timeout (<code>runMcpStdioServer</code>, <code>:78-100</code>):</p>
<ul>
<li>Default idle shutdown: 10 minutes (<code>DEFAULT_IDLE_TIMEOUT_MS</code>)</li>
<li>Handles <code>notifications/initialized</code>, <code>ping</code>, tool list/call</li>
<li>Unknown methods → <code>-32601 Method not found</code></li>
</ul>
<hr>
<h2>6. LSP MCP tool catalog</h2>
<p>Registered tools (<code>tools.ts:560-669</code>):</p>

<p>Tool dispatch:</p>
<pre><code class="language-typescript">// 161_lazycodex/plugins/omo/components/lsp/packages/lsp-tools-mcp/src/tools.ts:547-549
const tool = LSP_MCP_TOOLS.find((candidate) => matchesToolName(candidate, name));
if (!tool) throw new Error(`Unknown LSP tool: ${name}`);
return tool.execute(params, signal);
</code></pre>
<p><code>rename</code> description explicitly states it applies workspace edits (<code>:656-657</code>) — filesystem mutation via LSP protocol, not Codex <code>apply_patch</code>.</p>
<hr>
<h2>7. Language server subprocess spawning</h2>
<pre><code class="language-typescript">// 161_lazycodex/plugins/omo/components/lsp/packages/lsp-tools-mcp/src/lsp/process.ts:24-28,148-161
export interface PreparedSpawnCommand {
  command: string;
  args: string[];
  shell: false;  // explicit — no shell interpolation
}
// ...
if (platform !== "win32") {
  return { command: cmd, args, shell: false };
}
</code></pre>
<p>Spawn preparation:</p>
<ul>
<li>Validates cwd exists and is directory (<code>validateCwd</code>, <code>:41-57</code>)</li>
<li>Windows: resolves <code>.cmd</code>/<code>.bat</code> shims without <code>shell: true</code> (<code>:112-172</code>)</li>
<li>Process tree kill on shutdown (<code>killProcessTree</code>, <code>:89-110</code>)</li>
<li><strong>Not a sandbox</strong> — runs configured LSP commands from project/user LSP config</li>
</ul>
<hr>
<h2>8. Workspace edit application (rename tool)</h2>
<pre><code class="language-typescript">// 161_lazycodex/plugins/omo/components/lsp/packages/lsp-tools-mcp/src/lsp/workspace-edit.ts:59-79
export function applyWorkspaceEdit(edit: WorkspaceEdit | null): ApplyResult {
  if (!edit) {
    return { success: false, filesModified: [], totalEdits: 0, errors: ["No edit provided"] };
  }
  if (edit.changes) {
    for (const [uri, edits] of Object.entries(edit.changes)) {
      const filePath = uriToPath(uri);
      const applyResult = applyTextEditsToFile(filePath, edits);
      // ...
    }
  }
}
</code></pre>
<p><code>applyTextEditsToFile</code> reads/writes files directly (<code>:19-48</code>). Also handles <code>documentChanges</code> create/rename/delete (<code>:81+</code>). This is the highest-risk tool surface in LC — relies on Codex MCP approval + host sandbox.</p>
<hr>
<h2>9. PostToolUse quality hooks — pseudo-tools</h2>
<h3>Comment checker</h3>
<pre><code class="language-typescript">// 161_lazycodex/plugins/omo/components/comment-checker/src/codex-hook.ts:35-65
export async function runCommentCheckerPostToolUse(...) {
  const requests = extractCodexCommentCheckRequests(input);
  if (requests.length === 0) return "";
  // ...
  return JSON.stringify({
    decision: "block",
    reason: formatWarnings(warnings),
  });
}
</code></pre>
<p>Extracts file paths from Codex tool input/response (<code>extractCodexCommentCheckRequests</code>, <code>:31-33</code>). Blocks when AI-slop comment patterns detected.</p>
<h3>LSP diagnostics hook</h3>
<pre><code class="language-typescript">// 161_lazycodex/plugins/omo/components/lsp/src/codex-hook.ts:27-33,36-48
const MUTATION_TOOL_NAMES = new Set(["apply_patch", "write", "edit", "multiedit", "multi_edit"]);

export async function runLspPostToolUseHook(...) {
  const filePaths = extractMutatedFilePaths(input);
  if (filePaths.length === 0) return "";
  // run diagnostics per file; block if errors remain
}
</code></pre>
<p>Uses same underlying <code>executeLspDiagnostics</code> as MCP tool (<code>:31-33</code>) but triggered automatically post-edit — model did not invoke the tool explicitly.</p>
<hr>
<h2>10. Rules hook — context not dispatch</h2>
<p>Rules <code>PostToolUse</code> emits <code>additionalContext</code> for matched files — does not register as an MCP tool or model-callable function. See <code>002_prompt-context/02_lc_prompt.md</code>.</p>
<hr>
<h2>11. Ultrawork / ultragoal — no tool registration</h2>
<ul>
<li><code>ultrawork-detector.py</code> — stdout context injection only; exit 0 always</li>
<li><code>ultragoal</code> — may mutate <code>.omo/</code> goal files via steering CLI; not in MCP registry</li>
</ul>
<p>Subagent spawn tools (<code>spawn_agent</code>, <code>wait_agent</code>) are <strong>Codex host builtins</strong>, not LC-registered. LC bundles TOML agent role definitions under <code>components/ultrawork/agents/</code> for host consumption.</p>
<hr>
<h2>12. OmO submodule tool registry (OpenCode — reference)</h2>
<p>Upstream OmO in <code>161_lazycodex/src/</code> implements full tool factories:</p>
<pre><code>src/src/tools/index.ts
src/src/tools/skill/tools.ts
src/src/tools/delegate-task/
src/src/tools/call-omo-agent/
src/src/plugin/tool-registry.ts
</code></pre>
<p>These register OpenCode-native tools (<code>call_omo_agent</code>, <code>task</code>, <code>background_output</code>). <strong>Not active</strong> on Codex platform — LC Codex path uses host tools + LSP MCP only. Skill sync rewrites OpenCode examples to Codex equivalents (<code>sync-skills.mjs:18-30</code>).</p>

<hr>
<h2>16. Security notes</h2>
<ul>
<li><strong>LSP config trust</strong>: User/project LSP server commands execute with <code>shell: false</code> but full user privileges</li>
<li><strong><code>lsp.rename</code></strong>: Can modify multiple files via workspace edit — requires Codex tool approval</li>
<li><strong>Hook subprocesses</strong>: Run as user; inherit environment; no seccomp/seatbelt in LC</li>
<li><strong>No network MCP</strong>: LC snapshot registers LSP only — reduces MCP SSRF surface vs OmO OpenCode full stack</li>
<li><strong>Telemetry</strong>: Separate outbound PostHog — not a model tool (<code>components/telemetry/</code>)</li>
</ul>
<hr>
<h2>17. Test coverage</h2>
<pre><code class="language-javascript">// 161_lazycodex/plugins/omo/test/aggregate.test.mjs:60-71
// MCP lsp server path isolation

// 161_lazycodex/src/packages/lsp-tools-mcp/test/mcp.test.ts (submodule)
// JSON-RPC request/response unit tests
</code></pre>
<p>Component-level tests exist under each <code>components/*/test/</code> directory.</p>
<hr>
<h2>18. Operational workflow</h2>
<ol>
<li>Codex session loads <code>omo</code> plugin → reads <code>.mcp.json</code> → spawns LSP MCP on first tool need</li>
<li>Model calls <code>lsp_diagnostics</code> / <code>lsp_goto_definition</code> via MCP</li>
<li>MCP server spawns language server for file extension (from LSP config)</li>
<li>User edits via <code>apply_patch</code> → PostToolUse hooks fire automatically</li>
<li>LSP hook may block with error diagnostics; comment-checker may block on slop comments</li>
<li>Rules hook may inject dynamic context for edited files</li>
<li>MCP server idles out after 10 minutes if unused</li>
</ol>
<hr>

3a:T57e4,<h2>기초 설명</h2>
<p>LazyCodex exposes skills through the bundled <code>omo</code> Codex plugin: manifest path <code>./skills/</code>, build-time sync from component and shared sources, Codex compatibility rewrites for OpenCode orchestration examples, and marketplace registration under <code>sisyphuslabs</code>. Skill <strong>invocation</strong> and lazy loading are Codex host behaviors.</p>

<h2>코퍼스 — 004_skill-system/04_lc_skill.md (심화)</h2>
<h1>LazyCodex — Skill System</h1>
<blockquote>
<p><strong>분석 스냅샷</strong>: <code>/Users/jun/Developer/codex/161_lazycodex/</code> — <strong>packaging and distribution</strong> of OmO-derived skills under one Codex plugin namespace; no native skill loader or activation engine.</p>
</blockquote>
<p>LazyCodex exposes skills through the bundled <code>omo</code> Codex plugin: manifest path <code>./skills/</code>, build-time sync from component and shared sources, Codex compatibility rewrites for OpenCode orchestration examples, and marketplace registration under <code>sisyphuslabs</code>. Skill <strong>invocation</strong> and lazy loading are Codex host behaviors.</p>
<h2>Architecture</h2>
<pre><code class="language-mermaid">flowchart TD
  Build["npm run build"] --> Sync["sync-skills.mjs"]
  Sync --> Comp["Component skills&#x3C;br/>comment-checker, lsp, rules, ultragoal"]
  Sync --> Shared["shared-skills/skills/*&#x3C;br/>(when present)"]
  Sync --> Adapt["insertCodexCompatibilityGuidance"]
  Adapt --> Out["plugins/omo/skills/"]
  Out --> Manifest["plugin.json skills: ./skills/"]
  Manifest --> CX["Codex host lazy-load"]
  Market[".agents/plugins/marketplace.json"] --> CX
  Agents["ultrawork/agents/*.toml"] -.->|"referenced by skills"| Out
</code></pre>
<hr>
<h2>1. Role in the LazyCodex stack</h2>
<pre><code class="language-javascript">// 161_lazycodex/bin/lazycodex-ai.js:9-10
forwardedArgs[0] === "install"
  ? ["--package", "oh-my-openagent", "omo", "install", "--platform=codex", ...]
</code></pre>
<p>Install deploys the aggregate plugin (including skills) to the user's Codex config. The shim does not parse or execute skills at runtime.</p>
<p>Plugin manifest:</p>
<pre><code class="language-json">// 161_lazycodex/plugins/omo/.codex-plugin/plugin.json:14,27-31
"skills": "./skills/",
"defaultPrompt": [
  "Use OMO LSP diagnostics on this workspace.",
  "Show which OMO rules matched this file.",
  "ulw: run this change with evidence."
]
</code></pre>
<p><code>defaultPrompt</code> entries are marketplace starter prompts — not automatic skill injection.</p>
<hr>
<h2>2. Marketplace packaging</h2>
<pre><code class="language-json">// 161_lazycodex/.agents/plugins/marketplace.json:1-16
{
  "name": "sisyphuslabs",
  "interface": { "displayName": "Sisyphus Labs" },
  "plugins": [{
    "name": "omo",
    "source": "./plugins/omo",
    "category": "Developer Tools",
    "policy": {
      "installation": "AVAILABLE",
      "authentication": "ON_INSTALL"
    }
  }]
}
</code></pre>
<p>Single plugin namespace <code>omo</code> aggregates all component skills — users install one marketplace entry, not per-component plugins.</p>
<hr>
<h2>3. Build pipeline — sync-skills.mjs</h2>
<h3>Source mapping</h3>
<pre><code class="language-javascript">// 161_lazycodex/plugins/omo/scripts/sync-skills.mjs:6-14
const root = dirname(dirname(fileURLToPath(import.meta.url)));
const sharedSkillsRoot = join(root, "..", "..", "shared-skills", "skills");
const skillsRoot = join(root, "skills");
const skillSources = [
  ["comment-checker", "components/comment-checker/skills/comment-checker"],
  ["lsp", "components/lsp/skills/lsp"],
  ["rules", "components/rules/skills/rules"],
  ["ultragoal", "components/ultragoal/skills/ultragoal"],
];
</code></pre>
<p>Build steps (<code>:57-74</code>):</p>
<ol>
<li><code>rm -rf skills/</code> — clean regenerate</li>
<li>Copy each component skill directory</li>
<li>Run <code>adaptSkillForCodex</code> (compatibility injection)</li>
<li>Copy all directories from <code>shared-skills/skills/</code> when present</li>
<li>Adapt shared skills too</li>
</ol>
<p>Triggered by package build:</p>
<pre><code class="language-json">// 161_lazycodex/plugins/omo/package.json:17-20
"build": "node scripts/sync-skills.mjs &#x26;&#x26; node ../scripts/sync-telemetry-component.mjs &#x26;&#x26; npm run build --workspaces --if-present",
"sync:skills": "node scripts/sync-skills.mjs",
</code></pre>
<hr>

<hr>
<h2>5. Codex harness tool compatibility rewrite</h2>
<p>OpenCode-only tool names in skill examples trigger automatic preamble injection:</p>
<pre><code class="language-javascript">// 161_lazycodex/plugins/omo/scripts/sync-skills.mjs:16-34
const opencodeOnlyOrchestrationPattern = /\b(?:call_omo_agent|background_output|team_[a-z_]+|task)\s*\(/;

const codexHarnessToolCompatibility = `## Codex Harness Tool Compatibility
...
| \`call_omo_agent(subagent_type="explore", ...)\` | \`spawn_agent(agent_type="explorer", ...)\` |
| \`call_omo_agent(subagent_type="librarian", ...)\` | \`spawn_agent(agent_type="librarian", ...)\` |
| \`task(subagent_type="plan", ...)\` | \`spawn_agent(agent_type="plan", ...)\` |
| \`task(subagent_type="oracle", ...)\` for final verification | \`spawn_agent(agent_type="codex-ultrawork-reviewer", ...)\` |
| \`background_output(task_id="...")\` | \`wait_agent(...)\` |
| \`team_*(...)\` | Codex native subagents + send_message, followup_task, wait_agent, close_agent |
`;
</code></pre>
<p>Insertion logic (<code>:36-45</code>):</p>
<ul>
<li>Skip if pattern not found or block already present</li>
<li>Insert after YAML frontmatter if present; else prepend to file</li>
</ul>
<p><strong>Rule</strong>: When skill body conflicts with compatibility section, compatibility section wins (<code>sync-skills.mjs:32</code>).</p>
<hr>
<h2>6. Bundled Codex agent TOMLs (skill cross-references)</h2>
<p>Skills referencing subagent types must match bundled TOML definitions:</p>
<pre><code>161_lazycodex/plugins/omo/components/ultrawork/agents/
├── explorer.toml
├── librarian.toml
├── plan.toml
└── codex-ultrawork-reviewer.toml
</code></pre>
<p><code>aggregate.test.mjs</code> verifies:</p>
<ul>
<li>All four TOML files exist</li>
<li>Skills with <code>spawn_agent(agent_type="...")</code> references have matching TOML <code>name</code> field</li>
<li><code>findSpawnAgentTypes</code> regex extracts agent types from skill content (<code>:13-19</code>)</li>
</ul>
<p>Example agent definition consumed by skills:</p>
<pre><code class="language-toml"># 161_lazycodex/plugins/omo/components/ultrawork/agents/explorer.toml:1-6
name = "explorer"
description = "Codebase search specialist for Codex sessions..."
model = "gpt-5.4-mini"
model_reasoning_effort = "low"
</code></pre>
<p>Skills teach <strong>when</strong> to spawn these roles; Codex host executes <code>spawn_agent</code>.</p>
<hr>
<h2>7. Skill format — SKILL.md conventions</h2>
<p>Component skills follow standard frontmatter + markdown body pattern. After sync, Codex-compatible skills may include:</p>
<ol>
<li>YAML frontmatter (name, description, triggers)</li>
<li><code>## Codex Harness Tool Compatibility</code> block (if OpenCode examples detected)</li>
<li>Procedure body with tool examples translated to Codex names</li>
</ol>
<p>Lazy loading: Codex reads skill metadata from plugin manifest; full <code>SKILL.md</code> body loads when model/user activates skill — <strong>not</strong> merged into every system prompt.</p>
<hr>
<h2>8. OmO upstream skill runtime (OpenCode — reference)</h2>
<p>Submodule <code>161_lazycodex/src/</code> implements OpenCode-native skill tools:</p>
<pre><code>src/src/tools/skill/tools.ts
src/src/tools/skill/description-formatter.ts
src/src/plugin/skill-context.ts
src/src/shared/host-skill-config.ts
</code></pre>
<p>OpenCode path registers <code>skill</code> tools in plugin tool registry (<code>src/src/plugin/tool-registry.ts</code>). <strong>Codex platform install does not use this registry</strong> — skills are static files in <code>./skills/</code> consumed by Codex host API.</p>

<hr>
<h2>13. Maintainer workflow</h2>
<ol>
<li>Edit skill source in <code>components/*/skills/</code> or upstream <code>shared-skills/</code></li>
<li>Run <code>npm run sync:skills</code> in <code>plugins/omo/</code></li>
<li>Review generated <code>skills/</code> for compatibility block correctness</li>
<li>Run <code>npm test</code> — aggregate + sync-skills tests</li>
<li>Release via LC/OmO publish pipeline → user <code>lazycodex-ai install</code> updates plugin</li>
</ol>
<hr>
<h2>14. Design boundary</h2>
<p>Do not document LazyCodex as implementing:</p>
<ul>
<li>Skill embedding / vector search</li>
<li>Skill activation classifiers (model-side)</li>
<li>Skill permission policies (beyond Codex host)</li>
<li>Runtime skill hot-reload (requires plugin reinstall / host refresh)</li>
</ul>
<p>LC is a <strong>skill packager</strong> for Codex plugin distribution.</p>
<hr>

<td>Compatibility block prepended to entire file</td>
</tr>

<td>Unknown spawn_agent type in skill</td>

</tr>

</tr>

3b:T570c,<h2>기초 설명</h2>
<p>LazyCodex packages four Codex agent role definitions (<code>explorer</code>, <code>librarian</code>, <code>plan</code>, <code>codex-ultrawork-reviewer</code>), ultrawork keyword workflow injection, and skill-level Codex compatibility mappings. Process isolation, async scheduling, and inter-agent messaging are Codex runtime concerns.</p>
<h2>이 문서에서 다루는 것</h2>

<h2>소스 코드 스니펫</h2>
<h3>README / docs</h3>
<pre><code class="language-mermaid">flowchart TD
  User["User prompt with ulw/ultrawork"] --> Det["ultrawork-detector.py"]
  Det --> Ctx["additional_context directive"]
  Ctx --> Orch["Orchestrator agent"]
  Orch --> SA["Codex spawn_agent"]
  SA --> E["explorer — read-only search"]
  SA --> L["librarian — external OSS research"]
  SA --> P["plan — plan-only markdown"]
  SA --> W["worker — implementation"]
  SA --> R["codex-ultrawork-reviewer — gate"]
  R -->|REJECTION| Orch
  R -->|APPROVAL| Done["Done"]
  TOML["agents/*.toml"] -.-> SA
  Skills["skills/ spawn_agent examples"] -.-> Orch
</code></pre>

function findSpawnAgentTypes(content) {
  const agentTypes = new Set();
  const regex = /spawn_agent\(agent_type="([^"]+)"/g;
  for (const match of content.matchAll(regex)) {
    agentTypes.add(match[1]);
  }

}

<h2>코퍼스 — 005_subagents-collab/05_lc_subagent.md (심화)</h2>
<h1>LazyCodex — Subagents / Collaboration</h1>
<blockquote>
<p><strong>분석 스냅샷</strong>: <code>/Users/jun/Developer/codex/161_lazycodex/</code> — <strong>no standalone subagent scheduler</strong>; collaboration via Codex host spawn APIs + bundled OmO ultrawork TOML roles and prompt hooks.</p>
</blockquote>
<p>LazyCodex packages four Codex agent role definitions (<code>explorer</code>, <code>librarian</code>, <code>plan</code>, <code>codex-ultrawork-reviewer</code>), ultrawork keyword workflow injection, and skill-level Codex compatibility mappings. Process isolation, async scheduling, and inter-agent messaging are Codex runtime concerns.</p>
<h2>Architecture</h2>
<pre><code class="language-mermaid">flowchart TD
  User["User prompt with ulw/ultrawork"] --> Det["ultrawork-detector.py"]
  Det --> Ctx["additional_context directive"]
  Ctx --> Orch["Orchestrator agent"]
  Orch --> SA["Codex spawn_agent"]
  SA --> E["explorer — read-only search"]
  SA --> L["librarian — external OSS research"]
  SA --> P["plan — plan-only markdown"]
  SA --> W["worker — implementation"]
  SA --> R["codex-ultrawork-reviewer — gate"]
  R -->|REJECTION| Orch
  R -->|APPROVAL| Done["Done"]
  TOML["agents/*.toml"] -.-> SA
  Skills["skills/ spawn_agent examples"] -.-> Orch
</code></pre>
<hr>

<hr>
<h2>2. Bundled Codex agent roles</h2>
<p>Four TOML files under <code>plugins/omo/components/ultrawork/agents/</code>:</p>
<h3>explorer — read-only codebase search</h3>
<pre><code class="language-toml"># 161_lazycodex/plugins/omo/components/ultrawork/agents/explorer.toml:1-6,65-67
name = "explorer"
description = "Codebase search specialist for Codex sessions..."
model = "gpt-5.4-mini"
# ...
# READ-ONLY. Tools I will NEVER call: edit, write, apply_patch, spawn_agent, call_*_agent
</code></pre>
<p>Output contract requires <code>&#x3C;analysis></code> and <code>&#x3C;results></code> blocks with <strong>absolute paths</strong> (<code>:24-46</code>). Tool strategy: parallel LSP + ripgrep + ast_grep (<code>:48-56</code>).</p>
<h3>librarian — external OSS / docs research</h3>
<pre><code class="language-toml"># 161_lazycodex/plugins/omo/components/ultrawork/agents/librarian.toml:1-6,11-17
name = "librarian"
description = "External open-source codebase and documentation researcher..."
# USE me when: unfamiliar package, upstream API, OSS implementation search
# AVOID me when: answer is in local working tree (explorer's job)
</code></pre>
<p>Uses host <code>web_search</code>, <code>webfetch</code>, <code>gh</code> CLI per instructions (<code>:42+</code>). SHA-pinned GitHub permalink citations required.</p>
<h3>plan — strategic planner (no product code)</h3>
<pre><code class="language-toml"># 161_lazycodex/plugins/omo/components/ultrawork/agents/plan.toml:1-6,11-17
name = "plan"
# You ARE the planner. You ARE NOT an implementer.
# When caller demands implementation, REFUSE.
</code></pre>
<p>Phase 1 mandates parallel read-only subagents before drafting (<code>:26-34</code>):</p>
<pre><code>Spawn parallel read-only subagents for internal-source aspects...
Spawn parallel read-only subagents for external-source aspects...
</code></pre>
<p>Plan output: single <code>plans/&#x3C;slug>.md</code> with waves, dependency matrix, QA scenarios (<code>:36-141</code>).</p>
<h3>codex-ultrawork-reviewer — verification gate</h3>
<pre><code class="language-toml"># 161_lazycodex/plugins/omo/components/ultrawork/agents/codex-ultrawork-reviewer.toml:1-17
name = "codex-ultrawork-reviewer"
description = "Strict ultrawork verification reviewer..."
# Return UNCONDITIONAL APPROVAL only when diff satisfies every success criterion
# Return REJECTION if any criterion lacks evidence
</code></pre>
<p>Strict binary verdict — "looks good but..." counts as rejection (<code>:14-16</code>).</p>
<hr>
<h2>3. Ultrawork keyword trigger</h2>
<pre><code class="language-python"># 161_lazycodex/plugins/omo/components/ultrawork/hooks/ultrawork-detector.py:21-22,276-290
ULTRAWORK_PATTERN = re.compile(r"\b(?:ultrawork|ulw)\b", re.IGNORECASE)

def main() -> None:
    payload = _load_payload()
    if payload is not None and _should_inject(payload):
        _ = sys.stdout.write(ULTRAWORK_DIRECTIVE)
    sys.exit(0)
</code></pre>
<p>Registered on <code>UserPromptSubmit</code> (<code>hooks.json:35-42</code>), timeout 5s.</p>
<p>Directive highlights (<code>ULTRAWORK_DIRECTIVE</code>, <code>:25-256</code>):</p>
<ul>
<li>First visible line: <code>ULTRAWORK MODE ENABLED!</code></li>
<li>Requires test-first RED→GREEN <strong>and</strong> manual QA via HTTP/tmux/browser/computer-use channels</li>
<li>Mandates <code>create_goal</code> or binding <code># Goal</code> block with success criteria</li>
<li>Requires spawning reviewer before declaring done</li>
<li>Parallel exploration stop rules after 2 unproductive waves</li>
</ul>
<p>Hook <strong>never blocks</strong> (exit 0 always) — collaboration mode is advisory injection, not permission gate.</p>
<hr>
<h2>4. Codex-native spawn mapping (from skills sync)</h2>
<p>OpenCode examples in skills are rewritten for Codex:</p>
<pre><code class="language-javascript">// 161_lazycodex/plugins/omo/scripts/sync-skills.mjs:24-30
| `call_omo_agent(subagent_type="explore", ...)` | `spawn_agent(agent_type="explorer", ...)` |
| `call_omo_agent(subagent_type="librarian", ...)` | `spawn_agent(agent_type="librarian", ...)` |
| `task(subagent_type="plan", ...)` | `spawn_agent(agent_type="plan", ...)` |
| `task(subagent_type="oracle", ...)` for final verification | `spawn_agent(agent_type="codex-ultrawork-reviewer", ...)` |
| `task(category="...", ...)` for implementation | `spawn_agent(agent_type="worker", ...)` |
| `background_output(task_id="...")` | `wait_agent(...)` |
| `team_*(...)` | send_message, followup_task, wait_agent, close_agent |
</code></pre>
<p><code>worker</code> agent type referenced for implementation tasks — may be Codex default worker, not a bundled TOML in ultrawork/agents/ (only four TOMLs checked in).</p>
<hr>
<h2>5. Collaboration workflow (ultrawork mode)</h2>
<ol>
<li>User includes <code>ulw</code> or <code>ultrawork</code> in prompt</li>
<li>Detector injects full workflow directive into turn context</li>
<li>Orchestrator creates goal with success criteria</li>
<li><strong>Parallel phase</strong>: spawn <code>explorer</code> (internal) + <code>librarian</code> (external) read-only agents</li>
<li>Optional: spawn <code>plan</code> for large/ambiguous work → <code>plans/&#x3C;slug>.md</code></li>
<li>Implementation via <code>worker</code> spawn(s) or orchestrator direct edits</li>
<li>Manual QA scenarios per criterion (HTTP/tmux/browser/CU)</li>
<li>Spawn <code>codex-ultrawork-reviewer</code> with diff + evidence</li>
<li>Reviewer returns APPROVAL or REJECTION with blocking issues</li>
<li>Loop until approval or user intervention</li>
</ol>
<p>LC defines <strong>roles and prompt discipline</strong>; Codex executes spawns and carries messages.</p>
<hr>
<h2>6. Test contract — TOML + skill alignment</h2>
<pre><code class="language-javascript">// 161_lazycodex/plugins/omo/test/aggregate.test.mjs:13-19
function findSpawnAgentTypes(content) {
  const agentTypes = new Set();
  const regex = /spawn_agent\(agent_type="([^"]+)"/g;
  for (const match of content.matchAll(regex)) {
    agentTypes.add(match[1]);
  }
  return [...agentTypes].sort();
}
</code></pre>
<p>Tests verify:</p>
<ul>
<li>Four agent TOML files exist with expected <code>name</code> fields</li>
<li>Skills referencing custom agent types have matching TOML definitions</li>
<li>Hook commands stay under <code>components/</code> paths (<code>:38-57</code>)</li>
</ul>
<hr>
<h2>7. OmO upstream subagent runtime (OpenCode — reference)</h2>
<p>Submodule implements full delegation stack:</p>
<pre><code>161_lazycodex/src/src/tools/delegate-task/
161_lazycodex/src/src/tools/call-omo-agent/
161_lazycodex/src/src/tools/background-task/
161_lazycodex/src/src/shared/tmux/
</code></pre>
<p>OpenCode hooks include <code>delegate-task-retry</code>, <code>ralph-loop</code>, <code>start-work</code> (<code>create-session-hooks.ts:211-229</code>). README documents OpenCode commands <code>$ulw-loop</code>, <code>$ulw-plan</code>, <code>$start-work</code> (<code>README.md:46-52</code>) — <strong>OpenCode session features</strong>, not Codex plugin hooks.</p>
<p>Codex users get ultrawork via keyword + TOML roles, not <code>$ulw-loop</code> slash commands (unless Codex adds equivalent).</p>

<hr>
<h2>9. Parallelism model</h2>
<p>Plan agent specifies wave-based parallel execution (<code>plan.toml:64-80</code>):</p>
<ul>
<li>Target 5-8 tasks per wave</li>
<li>Wave 1 shared dependencies extracted first</li>
<li>Dependency matrix required in plan output</li>
</ul>
<p>Ultrawork directive mandates parallel subagent research before implementation. Actual concurrency limits are <strong>Codex host</strong> scheduler policies.</p>
<hr>
<h2>10. Review gate semantics</h2>
<p>Reviewer input expectation (<code>codex-ultrawork-reviewer.toml:10-11</code>):</p>
<blockquote>
<p>Input should include the goal, success criteria, full diff, QA evidence, and notepad path.</p>
</blockquote>
<p>Verdict strings:</p>
<ul>
<li><code>UNCONDITIONAL APPROVAL</code> — all criteria proven</li>
<li><code>REJECTION</code> — missing evidence, drift, or risk</li>
</ul>
<p>Ultrawork directive ties declaration-of-done to reviewer approval — process contract, not automated CI.</p>

<hr>
<h2>12. What LC does NOT implement</h2>
<ul>
<li>Subagent process isolation / cgroup</li>
<li>Cross-agent mailbox persistence (Codex host)</li>
<li>Automatic spawn scheduling / queue</li>
<li>Team topology (<code>team_*</code> — OpenCode only; mapped to Codex messages in skill sync)</li>
<li>Ralph loop / <code>$ulw-loop</code> on Codex (OpenCode feature in README)</li>
</ul>
<hr>
<h2>13. Security / trust notes</h2>
<ul>
<li>Spawned agents inherit orchestrator permission mode from Codex session</li>
<li>Read-only roles rely on prompt constraints — not hardware enforcement</li>
<li>Librarian agent may fetch arbitrary URLs via host web tools — SSRF boundary is Codex policy</li>
<li>Reviewer cannot block at OS level — only influences orchestrator via message</li>
</ul>

#!/usr/bin/env node
import { spawnSync } from "node:child_process"

const args = process.argv.slice(2)
const dryRun = args[0] === "--dry-run"
const forwardedArgs = dryRun ? args.slice(1) : args
const commandArgs =
  forwardedArgs[0] === "install"
    ? ["--package", "oh-my-openagent", "omo", "install", "--platform=codex", ...forwardedArgs.slice(1)]
    : ["--package", "oh-my-openagent", "omo", ...forwardedArgs]

if (dryRun) {
  console.log(["bunx", ...commandArgs].join(" "))
  process.exit(0)
}

const result = spawnSync("bunx", commandArgs, { stdio: "inherit" })
process.exit(result.status ?? 1)
</code></pre>

<h2>코퍼스 — 006_app-server-client-surfaces/06_lc_surface.md (심화)</h2>
<h1>LazyCodex — App Server / Client Surfaces</h1>
<blockquote>
<p><strong>분석 스냅샷</strong>: <code>/Users/jun/Developer/codex/161_lazycodex/</code> — <strong>not an agent app server</strong>; three concrete surfaces: npm CLI shim, bundled Codex plugin (hooks + LSP MCP stdio), and public Next.js docs on Cloudflare Workers.</p>
</blockquote>
<p>LazyCodex does not ship JSON-RPC session daemons, WebSocket streaming endpoints, REST APIs, or client SDKs for agent control. Agent session transport, tool streaming, and approvals are Codex/OmO host-owned. LC packages entrypoints and plugin components.</p>
<h2>Architecture</h2>
<pre><code class="language-mermaid">flowchart LR
  subgraph LC["LazyCodex-owned surfaces"]
    CLI["lazycodex-ai.js&#x3C;br/>npm bin"]
    Plugin["plugins/omo&#x3C;br/>Codex plugin"]
    MCP["LSP MCP stdio"]
    Web["packages/web&#x3C;br/>Next.js docs"]
  end
  subgraph Host["Not LC-owned"]
    CX["Codex CLI / IDE"]
    AS["codex-rs/app-server"]
  end
  User["User"] --> CLI
  CLI -->|install| Plugin
  User --> CX
  CX --> Plugin
  CX --> MCP
  User --> Web
  IDE["IDE clients"] --> AS
  AS -.->|"LC absent"| X["❌"]
</code></pre>
<hr>

<h2>2. CLI surface — synchronous forwarder</h2>
<pre><code class="language-javascript">// 161_lazycodex/bin/lazycodex-ai.js:1-27
#!/usr/bin/env node
import { spawnSync } from "node:child_process"

const args = process.argv.slice(2)
const dryRun = args[0] === "--dry-run"
const forwardedArgs = dryRun ? args.slice(1) : args
const commandArgs =
  forwardedArgs[0] === "install"
    ? ["--package", "oh-my-openagent", "omo", "install", "--platform=codex", ...forwardedArgs.slice(1)]
    : ["--package", "oh-my-openagent", "omo", ...forwardedArgs]

if (dryRun) {
  console.log(["bunx", ...commandArgs].join(" "))
  process.exit(0)
}

const result = spawnSync("bunx", commandArgs, { stdio: "inherit" })
process.exit(result.status ?? 1)
</code></pre>
<p>Characteristics:</p>
<ul>
<li><strong>No persistent server</strong> — one-shot process per invocation</li>
<li><strong><code>--dry-run</code></strong> prints resolved argv (<code>:13-15</code>) for CI/debug</li>
<li><strong><code>stdio: inherit</code></strong> — child owns terminal for install wizards</li>
<li>Install vs runtime distinguished by first arg (<code>:9-11</code>)</li>
</ul>
<p>README install entry:</p>
<pre><code class="language-bash"># 161_lazycodex/README.md:34-36
bunx lazycodex-ai install
# shorthand for bunx --package oh-my-openagent omo install --platform=codex
</code></pre>
<hr>
<h2>3. Codex plugin surface</h2>
<h3>Manifest</h3>
<pre><code class="language-json">// 161_lazycodex/plugins/omo/.codex-plugin/plugin.json:1-16
{
  "name": "omo",
  "skills": "./skills/",
  "hooks": "./hooks/hooks.json",
  "mcpServers": "./.mcp.json",
  "interface": {
    "displayName": "OMO",
    "capabilities": ["Hooks", "MCP Tools", "Code Intelligence", "Workflow", "Context Injection"]
  }
}
</code></pre>
<p>Codex host loads this at plugin install time — hooks register subprocess commands; MCP spawns on demand; skills expose directory to host skill API.</p>
<h3>Hook transport model</h3>
<p>Hooks are <strong>not</strong> network services — Codex spawns local subprocess per event:</p>
<pre><code class="language-json">// 161_lazycodex/plugins/omo/hooks/hooks.json:7-9
"command": "node \"${PLUGIN_ROOT}/components/rules/dist/cli.js\" hook session-start",
"timeout": 10,
"statusMessage": "loading OMO project rules"
</code></pre>
<p><code>${PLUGIN_ROOT}</code> resolved by Codex plugin loader. stdin JSON → stdout JSON/text. No HTTP, no WebSocket.</p>
<p>Aggregate test enforces component isolation:</p>
<pre><code class="language-javascript">// 161_lazycodex/plugins/omo/test/aggregate.test.mjs:38-57
// All hook paths must reference components/*/dist/cli.js — no external @scope packages
</code></pre>
<hr>
<h2>4. MCP surface — stdio JSON-RPC only</h2>
<pre><code class="language-json">// 161_lazycodex/plugins/omo/.mcp.json:1-9
{
  "mcpServers": {
    "lsp": {
      "command": "node",
      "args": ["./components/lsp/packages/lsp-tools-mcp/dist/cli.js", "mcp"],
      "cwd": "."
    }
  }
}
</code></pre>
<p>Server implementation:</p>
<pre><code class="language-typescript">// 161_lazycodex/plugins/omo/components/lsp/packages/lsp-tools-mcp/src/mcp.ts:78-82
export async function runMcpStdioServer(
  input: NodeJS.ReadableStream = process.stdin,
  output: NodeJS.WritableStream = process.stdout,
  options: McpStdioServerOptions = {},
): Promise&#x3C;void> {
</code></pre>
<p>Supported JSON-RPC methods (<code>:49-75</code>):</p>
<ul>
<li><code>initialize</code> — protocol handshake, <code>serverInfo: { name: "lsp", version: "0.1.0" }</code></li>
<li><code>tools/list</code> — seven LSP tools</li>
<li><code>tools/call</code> — execute tool</li>
<li><code>ping</code> — health check</li>
<li><code>notifications/initialized</code> — no response</li>
</ul>
<p><strong>No</strong> SSE MCP, <strong>no</strong> HTTP MCP, <strong>no</strong> websocket transport in LC snapshot.</p>
<p>Idle lifecycle: 10-minute default timeout closes server (<code>DEFAULT_IDLE_TIMEOUT_MS = 10 * 60_000</code>, <code>:46</code>).</p>
<hr>
<h2>5. Web surface — Next.js on Cloudflare Workers</h2>
<p>Repository layout from README:</p>
<pre><code># 161_lazycodex/README.md:84-91
lazycodex/
├── src/                     → oh-my-openagent (submodule)
├── packages/
│   └── web/                 → Next.js 15 + Tailwind v4 + opennextjs-cloudflare
│                              (deployed to lazycodex.ai via Cloudflare Workers)
├── .github/workflows/       → web-ci.yml + web-deploy.yml
</code></pre>
<p>Wrangler config:</p>
<pre><code class="language-toml"># 161_lazycodex/packages/web/wrangler.toml:1-18
main = ".open-next/worker.js"
name = "lazycodex-web"
compatibility_date = "2026-05-25"
compatibility_flags = ["nodejs_compat"]
workers_dev = false

[[routes]]
pattern = "lazycodex.ai"
custom_domain = true
</code></pre>
<p>Web surface is <strong>static/docs/marketing</strong> — not an agent control plane. No session API, no chat WebSocket, no tool streaming endpoint.</p>
<p>DNS note in wrangler: <code>www.lazycodex.ai</code>, <code>lazycodex.dev</code> redirect at Cloudflare edge — never hit Worker (<code>:12-15</code>).</p>
<p>Documentation URL referenced in README: <code>lazycodex.ai/docs</code> (<code>README.md:54</code>).</p>

<hr>
<h2>9. Client interaction model (Codex user)</h2>
<ol>
<li><strong>Install</strong>: <code>bunx lazycodex-ai install</code> → OmO writes Codex config + plugin files</li>
<li><strong>Session</strong>: User runs <strong><code>codex</code></strong> CLI or IDE — Codex is the client</li>
<li><strong>Plugin hooks</strong>: Codex invokes subprocess hooks on lifecycle events</li>
<li><strong>MCP</strong>: Codex spawns LSP MCP stdio child when model uses LSP tools</li>
<li><strong>Docs</strong>: Browser → <code>https://lazycodex.ai</code> for human documentation only</li>
</ol>
<p>LC never sits in the hot path of model streaming.</p>
<hr>

</code></pre>
<p>These are <strong>different product surfaces</strong> from LazyCodex-on-Codex. README still mentions OpenCode commands (<code>$ulw-loop</code>, etc.) for OmO users (<code>README.md:46-52</code>).</p>
