<hr>
<h2>13. Protocol details — LSP MCP stdio framing</h2>
<p>Request handling (<code>mcp.ts:49-76</code>):</p>
<ul>
<li>Malformed input → <code>-32600 Invalid Request</code></li>
<li>Unknown method → <code>-32601 Method not found</code></li>
<li>Tool errors returned in result with <code>isError: true</code> (handleToolCall path)</li>
</ul>
<p>Readline-based message loop on stdin — standard MCP stdio convention. Codex host manages process lifetime.</p>
<hr>
<h2>14. Security / exposure</h2>
<ul>
<li><strong>CLI</strong>: Runs <code>bunx</code> with user privileges — trusts npm registry for <code>oh-my-openagent</code></li>
<li><strong>Hooks</strong>: Subprocess with inherited env — no network bind</li>
<li><strong>MCP</strong>: Local stdio only — not exposed on TCP port by default</li>
<li><strong>Web</strong>: Public static docs — no agent credentials</li>
<li><strong>Telemetry</strong>: Outbound PostHog from telemetry hook — separate from user-facing surface</li>
</ul>

3d:T6203,<h2>기초 설명</h2>
<p>LazyCodex does not implement seatbelt, bwrap, seccomp, landlock, chroot, Docker sandboxes, network allowlists, or command classifiers. Policy surfaces are limited to: hook subprocess timeouts, post-edit <strong>block</strong> decisions (comment-checker, LSP), LSP language-server spawn with <code>shell: false</code>, and outbound telemetry opt-out flags.</p>

export function validateCwd(cwd: string): { valid: boolean; error?: string } {
  if (!existsSync(cwd)) {
    return { valid: false, error: `Working directory does not exist: ${cwd}` };
  }
  const stats = statSync(cwd);
  if (!stats.isDirectory()) {
    return { valid: false, error: `Path is not a directory: ${cwd}` };
  }
  return { valid: true };
}
</code></pre>
<h3>README / docs</h3>
<pre><code class="language-typescript">// 161_lazycodex/plugins/omo/components/lsp/packages/lsp-tools-mcp/src/lsp/process.ts:89-110
function killProcessTree(proc: ChildProcess, signal: NodeJS.Signals): void {
  if (process.platform === "win32" &#x26;&#x26; proc.pid) {
    spawnSync("taskkill", ["/pid", String(proc.pid), "/f", "/t"], { stdio: "ignore" });
  }
  if (process.platform !== "win32" &#x26;&#x26; proc.pid) {
    process.kill(-proc.pid, signal);  // process group
  }
}
</code></pre>

<h2>코퍼스 — 007_sandbox-exec-policy/07_lc_sandbox.md (심화)</h2>
<h1>LazyCodex — Sandbox / Exec Policy</h1>
<blockquote>
<p><strong>분석 스냅샷</strong>: <code>/Users/jun/Developer/codex/161_lazycodex/</code> — <strong>no OS-level sandbox or execution policy engine</strong>; thin npm wrapper + Codex plugin bundle delegating isolation to Codex host and tool approval flows.</p>
</blockquote>
<p>LazyCodex does not implement seatbelt, bwrap, seccomp, landlock, chroot, Docker sandboxes, network allowlists, or command classifiers. Policy surfaces are limited to: hook subprocess timeouts, post-edit <strong>block</strong> decisions (comment-checker, LSP), LSP language-server spawn with <code>shell: false</code>, and outbound telemetry opt-out flags.</p>
<h2>Architecture</h2>
<pre><code class="language-mermaid">flowchart TD
  subgraph LC["LC policy surfaces"]
    HookT["Hook timeouts&#x3C;br/>hooks.json"]
    Block["PostToolUse blocks&#x3C;br/>comment-checker, LSP"]
    LSPSpawn["LSP spawn shell:false"]
    Tel["Telemetry opt-out&#x3C;br/>env flags"]
  end
  subgraph Host["Codex host (not LC)"]
    SB["OS sandbox / seatbelt"]
    Guard["Tool approval / guardian"]
    Perm["permission_mode"]
  end
  User["User session"] --> Host
  Host --> LC
  LSPSpawn --> LS["User-configured&#x3C;br/>language servers"]
  LS --> FS["Filesystem mutations&#x3C;br/>via lsp.rename"]
  Guard --> FS
  SB --> Shell["bash/shell tool"]
</code></pre>
<hr>
<h2>1. Distribution shim — no policy</h2>
<pre><code class="language-javascript">// 161_lazycodex/bin/lazycodex-ai.js:18-20
const result = spawnSync("bunx", commandArgs, {
  stdio: "inherit",
})
</code></pre>
<ul>
<li>No argv filtering, no allowlist, no capability dropping</li>
<li>Inherits user UID/GID, full environment, network stack</li>
<li>Trust boundary: npm package <code>oh-my-openagent</code> from registry</li>
</ul>
<hr>
<h2>2. Hook subprocess policy</h2>
<h3>Timeouts (Codex-enforced cancellation)</h3>
<pre><code class="language-json">// 161_lazycodex/plugins/omo/hooks/hooks.json (selected)
SessionStart rules:     timeout 10
SessionStart telemetry: timeout 5
UserPromptSubmit rules: timeout 10
UserPromptSubmit ultrawork: timeout 5
UserPromptSubmit ultragoal: timeout 10
PostToolUse comment-checker: timeout 30
PostToolUse lsp:         timeout 60
PostToolUse rules:       timeout 10
PostCompact rules:       timeout 10
</code></pre>
<p>Hooks run as user subprocesses — no privilege separation from Codex process. Timeout is the primary <strong>resource bound</strong> LC configures.</p>
<h3>Ultrawork hook — never blocks</h3>
<pre><code class="language-python"># 161_lazycodex/plugins/omo/components/ultrawork/hooks/ultrawork-detector.py:10,290
# exit: 0 always (this hook never blocks the turn).
sys.exit(0)
</code></pre>
<p>Context injection only — not an execution gate.</p>
<hr>
<h2>3. Post-edit block policy</h2>
<h3>Comment checker</h3>
<pre><code class="language-typescript">// 161_lazycodex/plugins/omo/components/comment-checker/src/codex-hook.ts:60-65
return JSON.stringify({
  decision: "block",
  reason: formatWarnings(warnings),
});
</code></pre>
<p>Triggers on mutation tools matched in hooks.json (<code>apply_patch|write|edit|...</code>). Policy: <strong>block turn</strong> when AI-slop comment patterns detected in edited files. Skips on <code>missing</code>, <code>pass</code>, <code>error</code> statuses (<code>:52-53</code>).</p>
<p>This is <strong>quality policy</strong>, not OS sandbox — prevents proceeding with bad comments until addressed.</p>
<h3>LSP diagnostics hook</h3>
<pre><code class="language-typescript">// 161_lazycodex/plugins/omo/components/lsp/src/codex-hook.ts:27-28,55-57
const MUTATION_TOOL_NAMES = new Set(["apply_patch", "write", "edit", "multiedit", "multi_edit"]);
// ...
decision: "block",
reason,  // LSP error diagnostics after edit
</code></pre>
<p>Policy: block when <code>executeLspDiagnostics</code> reports errors (<code>severity: "error"</code>, <code>:31-33</code>) after successful mutation. Clean diagnostics or unsupported extension → no block (<code>CLEAN_DIAGNOSTICS_TEXT</code>, <code>UNSUPPORTED_EXTENSION_TEXT</code>, <code>:28-29</code>).</p>
<p>Both hooks return JSON consumed by Codex hook runtime — host decides how block affects tool loop.</p>
<hr>
<h2>4. LSP MCP — primary execution surface</h2>
<h3>Spawn policy — no shell</h3>
<pre><code class="language-typescript">// 161_lazycodex/plugins/omo/components/lsp/packages/lsp-tools-mcp/src/lsp/process.ts:24-28
export interface PreparedSpawnCommand {
  command: string;
  args: string[];
  shell: false;
}
</code></pre>
<pre><code class="language-typescript">// 161_lazycodex/plugins/omo/components/lsp/packages/lsp-tools-mcp/src/lsp/process.ts:159-161
if (platform !== "win32") {
  return { command: cmd, args, shell: false };
}
</code></pre>
<p>Windows resolves <code>.cmd</code>/<code>.bat</code> without <code>shell: true</code> (<code>:112-172</code>) — reduces shell injection risk but <strong>does not sandbox</strong> the LSP binary.</p>
<h3>Cwd validation</h3>
<pre><code class="language-typescript">// 161_lazycodex/plugins/omo/components/lsp/packages/lsp-tools-mcp/src/lsp/process.ts:41-57
export function validateCwd(cwd: string): { valid: boolean; error?: string } {
  if (!existsSync(cwd)) {
    return { valid: false, error: `Working directory does not exist: ${cwd}` };
  }
  const stats = statSync(cwd);
  if (!stats.isDirectory()) {
    return { valid: false, error: `Path is not a directory: ${cwd}` };
  }
  return { valid: true };
}
</code></pre>
<p>Invalid cwd → <code>LspInvalidPathError</code> at spawn (<code>:175-178</code>).</p>
<h3>Process tree termination</h3>
<pre><code class="language-typescript">// 161_lazycodex/plugins/omo/components/lsp/packages/lsp-tools-mcp/src/lsp/process.ts:89-110
function killProcessTree(proc: ChildProcess, signal: NodeJS.Signals): void {
  if (process.platform === "win32" &#x26;&#x26; proc.pid) {
    spawnSync("taskkill", ["/pid", String(proc.pid), "/f", "/t"], { stdio: "ignore" });
  }
  if (process.platform !== "win32" &#x26;&#x26; proc.pid) {
    process.kill(-proc.pid, signal);  // process group
  }
}
</code></pre>
<p>Cleanup policy on MCP idle timeout (10 min) or server shutdown — not a security boundary.</p>
<hr>
<h2>5. Filesystem mutation via LSP rename</h2>
<p>Highest-risk LC tool path:</p>
<pre><code class="language-typescript">// 161_lazycodex/plugins/omo/components/lsp/packages/lsp-tools-mcp/src/tools.ts:654-667
{
  name: "rename",
  aliases: ["lsp_rename"],
  description: "Rename a symbol across the workspace and apply the returned workspace edit.",
  // ...
}
</code></pre>
<p>Workspace edit application:</p>
<pre><code class="language-typescript">// 161_lazycodex/plugins/omo/components/lsp/packages/lsp-tools-mcp/src/lsp/workspace-edit.ts:19-48,59-79
function applyTextEditsToFile(filePath: string, edits: TextEdit[]): FileApplyResult {
  const content = readFileSync(filePath, "utf-8");
  // ... apply edits ...
  writeFileSync(filePath, lines.join("\n"), "utf-8");
}

export function applyWorkspaceEdit(edit: WorkspaceEdit | null): ApplyResult {
  // iterates edit.changes and edit.documentChanges — create/rename/delete supported
}
</code></pre>
<p><strong>Policy implication</strong>: Any file path LSP server returns in workspace edit can be modified. LC does not:</p>
<ul>
<li>Restrict paths to workspace root beyond LSP server behavior</li>
<li>Require secondary approval (relies on Codex MCP tool approval)</li>
<li>Snapshot/rollback filesystem state</li>
</ul>
<p>Language server commands come from <strong>user/project LSP config</strong> — untrusted config can specify arbitrary executables.</p>
<hr>
<h2>6. MCP server lifecycle bounds</h2>
<pre><code class="language-typescript">// 161_lazycodex/plugins/omo/components/lsp/packages/lsp-tools-mcp/src/mcp.ts:46,96-100
const DEFAULT_IDLE_TIMEOUT_MS = 10 * 60_000;
idleTimer = setTimeout(() => {
  closed = true;
  log("idle_timeout", { idle_timeout_ms: idleTimeoutMs });
  void options.onIdleTimeout?.();
}, idleTimeoutMs);
</code></pre>
<p>Resource policy: terminate idle MCP after 10 minutes. Not network egress control.</p>
<hr>
<h2>7. Telemetry — outbound network surface</h2>
<pre><code class="language-typescript">// 161_lazycodex/plugins/omo/components/telemetry/src/posthog.ts:6,32-35
import { shouldDisablePostHog } from "./env-flags.js";
const NO_OP_POSTHOG: PostHogClient = {
  trackActive: () => undefined,
  shutdown: async () => undefined,
};
</code></pre>
<p>Opt-out via environment flags (<code>shouldDisablePostHog</code>). When enabled, SessionStart hook sends anonymized activity to PostHog — <strong>not</strong> prompt content, but OS metadata (<code>getSharedProperties</code>, <code>:62-80</code>: platform, cpu, memory).</p>
<p>Telemetry is outbound network — separate from model tool policy. Users disable via env documented in component README/env-flags.</p>
<hr>
<h2>8. Rules hook — context only, no block</h2>
<p>Rules emit <code>additionalContext</code> — do not return <code>decision: block</code> in normal operation (<code>codex-hook.ts:455-462</code>). PostCompact clears cache only (<code>:104-110</code>).</p>
<p>Rules <strong>mode</strong> env config can disable injection (<code>mode === "off"</code>, <code>:136</code>, <code>:221</code>) — behavioral policy, not exec sandbox.</p>
<hr>
<h2>9. Ultragoal — filesystem writes to <code>.omo/</code></h2>
<pre><code class="language-typescript">// 161_lazycodex/plugins/omo/components/ultragoal/src/codex-hook.ts:25-31
const result = await steerUltragoal(payload.cwd, proposal);
</code></pre>
<p>Steering may write plan/ledger files under workspace <code>.omo/ultragoal</code> — user-project scoped, not system-wide. No path traversal audit documented in hook — trusts parsed steering syntax.</p>
<hr>
<h2>10. Codex host delegation (primary sandbox)</h2>
<p>LC explicitly relies on Codex for:</p>
<table>
<thead>
<tr>
<th>Concern</th>
<th>LC implementation</th>
</tr>
</thead>
<tbody>
<tr>
<td>Shell command sandbox</td>
<td><strong>None</strong> — Codex <code>shell</code> tool + seatbelt/sandbox</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>Network egress for bash</td>
<td><strong>None</strong> — Codex policy</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>MCP tool approval</td>
<td><strong>None</strong> — Codex guardian</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td><code>permission_mode</code></td>
<td>Passed to hooks in stdin JSON — host-owned</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>Subagent isolation</td>
<td><strong>None</strong> — Codex scheduler</td>
</tr>
</tbody>
</table>
<p>Hook inputs include <code>permission_mode</code> field (<code>codex-hook.ts:32</code>, <code>:43</code>, <code>:54</code>) — LC components can read but snapshot does not branch on it for sandbox behavior.</p>
<hr>
<h2>11. Absent mechanisms (negative evidence)</h2>
<p>Not found in <code>161_lazycodex/</code>:</p>
<table>
<thead>
<tr>
<th>Mechanism</th>
<th>Status</th>
</tr>
</thead>
<tbody>
<tr>
<td>seatbelt / sandbox-exec</td>
<td>Absent</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>bubblewrap / firejail</td>
<td>Absent</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>seccomp / landlock</td>
<td>Absent</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>Docker / container runtime</td>
<td>Absent</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>Network allow/deny lists</td>
<td>Absent</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>Command argv classifier</td>
<td>Absent</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>LC-owned approval protocol UI</td>
<td>Absent</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>Capability dropping (setuid/setgid)</td>
<td>Absent</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>Read-only root filesystem</td>
<td>Absent</td>
</tr>
</tbody>
</table>
<p>OmO submodule may implement additional OpenCode policies under <code>src/</code> — not bundled into Codex plugin exec path.</p>
<hr>
<h2>12. Threat model summary</h2>
<table>
<thead>
<tr>
<th>Threat</th>
<th>LC mitigation</th>
<th>Residual risk</th>
</tr>
</thead>
<tbody>
<tr>
<td>Malicious LSP server command in config</td>
<td><code>shell: false</code> spawn</td>
<td>Full user privileges</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td><code>lsp.rename</code> path traversal</td>
<td>None in LC</td>
<td>Codex approval + LSP server trust</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>Hook subprocess escape</td>
<td>Same user as Codex</td>
<td>Standard process trust model</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>Telemetry exfil</td>
<td>Opt-out flags</td>
<td>PostHog when enabled</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td><code>bunx</code> supply chain</td>
<td>None in LC</td>
<td>Trust npm + OmO package</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>AI editing bad comments</td>
<td>comment-checker block</td>
<td>Pattern-based, not exhaustive</td>
</tr>
</tbody>
</table>

<hr>
<h2>14. Operational guidance</h2>
<ol>
<li>Treat LSP config as <strong>trusted</strong> — it specifies executables run as your user</li>
<li>Use Codex permission modes and MCP approval for <code>lsp.rename</code></li>
<li>Disable telemetry if outbound analytics unacceptable (<code>shouldDisablePostHog</code>)</li>
<li>Rely on Codex sandbox for <code>shell</code>/<code>bash</code> — LC does not add layers</li>
<li>Ultrawork QA channels (HTTP/tmux/browser) in directive are <strong>orchestration policy</strong> — execution still under Codex tool policy</li>
</ol>

3e:T6a0c,<h2>기초 설명</h2>
<p>LazyCodex configuration is <strong>three-layer</strong>: (1) a zero-parser CLI shim, (2) a frozen marketplace snapshot under <code>.agents/plugins/</code>, and (3) component-local env/path knobs inside the bundled <code>plugins/omo</code> aggregate plugin. There is no <code>.lazycodexrc</code>, no layered settings merge, and no model-router config in this repository.</p>

export function configFromEnvironment(env: NodeJS.ProcessEnv = process.env): PiRulesConfig {
  const config = defaultConfig();
  const disableBundledRules = isTruthy(firstEnv(env, "CODEX_RULES_DISABLE_BUNDLED", "PI_RULES_DISABLE_BUNDLED"));
  config.disabled = isTruthy(firstEnv(env, "CODEX_RULES_DISABLED", "PI_RULES_DISABLED"));
  config.mode = parseMode(firstEnv(env, "CODEX_RULES_MODE", "PI_RULES_MODE")) ?? config.mode;
  config.maxRuleChars = parsePositiveInteger(firstEnv(env, "CODEX_RULES_MAX_RULE_CHARS", "PI_RULES_MAX_RULE_CHARS")) ?? config.maxRuleChars;
  config.maxResultChars = parsePositiveInteger(firstEnv(env, "CODEX_RULES_MAX_RESULT_CHARS", "PI_RULES_MAX_RESULT_CHARS")) ?? config.maxResultChars;
  config.enabledSources = parseEnabledSources(firstEnv(env, "CODEX_RULES_ENABLED_SOURCES", "PI_RULES_ENABLED_SOURCES"), disableBundledRules);
  return config;
}
</code></pre>

<h2>코퍼스 — 008_config-system/08_lc_config.md (심화)</h2>
<h1>LazyCodex Config System</h1>
<blockquote>
<p><strong>분석 스냅샷</strong>: <code>161_lazycodex/</code> — LazyCodex has <strong>no standalone config engine</strong>. It is a Codex Light distribution overlay: <code>lazycodex-ai</code> delegates to <code>oh-my-openagent omo install --platform=codex</code>, and real Codex TOML mutations are owned by the upstream OmO Codex installer.</p>
</blockquote>
<p>LazyCodex configuration is <strong>three-layer</strong>: (1) a zero-parser CLI shim, (2) a frozen marketplace snapshot under <code>.agents/plugins/</code>, and (3) component-local env/path knobs inside the bundled <code>plugins/omo</code> aggregate plugin. There is no <code>.lazycodexrc</code>, no layered settings merge, and no model-router config in this repository.</p>
<h2>Architecture</h2>
<pre><code class="language-mermaid">flowchart TD
  User["bunx lazycodex-ai install|run"] --> Shim["bin/lazycodex-ai.js"]
  Shim --> Bunx["bunx --package oh-my-openagent omo ..."]
  Bunx --> OmOInstall["omo install --platform=codex"]
  OmOInstall --> CodexHome["~/.codex/config.toml + marketplace cache"]
  CodexHome --> Plugin["omo@sisyphuslabs plugin activation"]
  Plugin --> CompEnv["components/* env + path config"]
  CompEnv --> Rules["CODEX_RULES_* / PI_RULES_*"]
  CompEnv --> LSP[".codex/lsp-client.json"]
  CompEnv --> Telemetry["POSTHOG opt-out + activity state dir"]
  CompEnv --> Ultragoal[".omo/ultragoal/*.json"]
</code></pre>
<hr>
<h2>1. CLI wrapper — argument forwarding only</h2>
<p>LazyCodex's only first-party executable parses argv and spawns <code>bunx</code>; it never reads TOML, JSON config, or env-based routing tables.</p>
<pre><code class="language-javascript">// 161_lazycodex/bin/lazycodex-ai.js:5-11
const args = process.argv.slice(2)
const dryRun = args[0] === "--dry-run"
const forwardedArgs = dryRun ? args.slice(1) : args
const commandArgs =
  forwardedArgs[0] === "install"
    ? ["--package", "oh-my-openagent", "omo", "install", "--platform=codex", ...forwardedArgs.slice(1)]
    : ["--package", "oh-my-openagent", "omo", ...forwardedArgs]
</code></pre>
<p><strong>Key behaviors:</strong></p>
<table>
<thead>
<tr>
<th>Behavior</th>
<th>Lines</th>
<th>Notes</th>
</tr>
</thead>
<tbody>
<tr>
<td>Install path injects <code>--platform=codex</code></td>
<td><code>:9-10</code></td>
<td>All Codex-specific config mutations happen inside OmO installer</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>Non-install forwards args verbatim</td>
<td><code>:11</code></td>
<td><code>bunx ... omo &#x3C;subcommand></code></td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td><code>--dry-run</code> prints command only</td>
<td><code>:13-15</code></td>
<td>No side effects; useful for CI/docs</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td><code>stdio: "inherit"</code></td>
<td><code>:18-19</code></td>
<td>User sees OmO TUI/output directly</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>Exit code passthrough</td>
<td><code>:27</code></td>
<td><code>result.status ?? 1</code></td>
</tr>
</tbody>
</table>
<p><strong>Boundary:</strong> Grep of <code>161_lazycodex/bin/</code> shows <strong>no</strong> <code>config</code>, <code>toml</code>, <code>readFile</code>, or settings parser — only <code>spawnSync</code> (<code>:18</code>).</p>
<hr>
<h2>2. Marketplace snapshot — <code>sisyphuslabs</code></h2>
<p>The repo ships a Codex marketplace manifest that pins the single <code>omo</code> plugin source path:</p>
<pre><code class="language-json">// 161_lazycodex/.agents/plugins/marketplace.json:1-16
{
  "name": "sisyphuslabs",
  "interface": { "displayName": "Sisyphus Labs" },
  "plugins": [{
    "name": "omo",
    "source": "./plugins/omo",
    "category": "Developer Tools",
    "policy": {
      "installation": "AVAILABLE",
      "authentication": "ON_INSTALL"
    }
  }]
}
</code></pre>
<table>
<thead>
<tr>
<th>Field</th>
<th>Role</th>
</tr>
</thead>
<tbody>
<tr>
<td><code>name: sisyphuslabs</code></td>
<td>Marketplace identity registered with Codex host</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td><code>source: ./plugins/omo</code></td>
<td>Relative path to aggregate plugin root in this checkout</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td><code>policy.installation: AVAILABLE</code></td>
<td>Plugin listed for install without extra gating in manifest</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td><code>policy.authentication: ON_INSTALL</code></td>
<td>Auth handshake deferred to install-time (host/OmO)</td>
</tr>
</tbody>
</table>
<p>LazyCodex does <strong>not</strong> implement marketplace CRUD APIs — it <strong>vends</strong> this JSON for OmO's <code>--platform=codex</code> installer to copy/register.</p>
<hr>
<h2>3. Aggregate plugin manifest — config surface pointers</h2>
<p>The <code>omo</code> plugin's <code>.codex-plugin/plugin.json</code> is the <strong>local config index</strong> for skills, hooks, and MCP:</p>
<pre><code class="language-json">// 161_lazycodex/plugins/omo/.codex-plugin/plugin.json:14-16
"skills": "./skills/",
"hooks": "./hooks/hooks.json",
"mcpServers": "./.mcp.json",
</code></pre>
<p>Additional interface metadata (<code>:17-33</code>) documents capabilities and default prompts but does not define runtime policy engines:</p>
<table>
<thead>
<tr>
<th>Capability (manifest)</th>

<hr>
<h2>5. Rules component — env-driven config</h2>
<p>Rules are the richest <strong>in-repo</strong> config surface. <code>configFromEnvironment</code> maps env vars to engine knobs:</p>
<pre><code class="language-typescript">// 161_lazycodex/plugins/omo/components/rules/src/config.ts:5-20
export function configFromEnvironment(env: NodeJS.ProcessEnv = process.env): PiRulesConfig {
  const config = defaultConfig();
  const disableBundledRules = isTruthy(firstEnv(env, "CODEX_RULES_DISABLE_BUNDLED", "PI_RULES_DISABLE_BUNDLED"));
  config.disabled = isTruthy(firstEnv(env, "CODEX_RULES_DISABLED", "PI_RULES_DISABLED"));
  config.mode = parseMode(firstEnv(env, "CODEX_RULES_MODE", "PI_RULES_MODE")) ?? config.mode;
  config.maxRuleChars = parsePositiveInteger(firstEnv(env, "CODEX_RULES_MAX_RULE_CHARS", "PI_RULES_MAX_RULE_CHARS")) ?? config.maxRuleChars;
  config.maxResultChars = parsePositiveInteger(firstEnv(env, "CODEX_RULES_MAX_RESULT_CHARS", "PI_RULES_MAX_RESULT_CHARS")) ?? config.maxResultChars;
  config.enabledSources = parseEnabledSources(firstEnv(env, "CODEX_RULES_ENABLED_SOURCES", "PI_RULES_ENABLED_SOURCES"), disableBundledRules);
  return config;
}
</code></pre>
<table>
<thead>
<tr>
<th>Env var(s)</th>
<th>Effect</th>
<th>Parser lines</th>
</tr>
</thead>
<tbody>
<tr>
<td><code>CODEX_RULES_DISABLED</code> / <code>PI_RULES_DISABLED</code></td>
<td>Master off switch</td>
<td><code>:8-9</code></td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td><code>CODEX_RULES_MODE</code> / <code>PI_RULES_MODE</code></td>
<td><code>static</code> | <code>dynamic</code> | <code>both</code> | <code>off</code></td>
<td><code>:38-49</code></td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td><code>CODEX_RULES_MAX_RULE_CHARS</code></td>
<td>Per-rule char budget</td>
<td><code>:52-55</code></td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td><code>CODEX_RULES_MAX_RESULT_CHARS</code></td>
<td>Injection size cap</td>
<td><code>:13-15</code></td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td><code>CODEX_RULES_ENABLED_SOURCES</code></td>
<td>Comma-separated source list or <code>auto</code></td>
<td><code>:58-72</code></td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td><code>CODEX_RULES_DISABLE_BUNDLED</code></td>
<td>Strips <code>plugin-bundled</code> from sources</td>
<td><code>:7, 75-76</code></td>
</tr>
</tbody>
</table>
<p>Session cache path (persistent dedupe state, not "memory extraction"):</p>
<pre><code class="language-typescript">// 161_lazycodex/plugins/omo/components/rules/src/persistent-cache.ts:75-77
export function sessionCachePath(sessionId: string, pluginDataRoot: string | undefined): string {
  const root = pluginDataRoot ?? process.env["PLUGIN_DATA"] ?? join(homedir(), ".codex", "codex-rules");
  return join(root, "sessions", `${safePathSegment(sessionId)}.json`);
}
</code></pre>
<p>Default on-disk layout: <code>~/.codex/codex-rules/sessions/&#x3C;sessionId>.json</code> unless <code>PLUGIN_DATA</code> overrides.</p>
<hr>
<h2>6. LSP component — client config paths</h2>
<p>LSP MCP and post-edit hooks consume LSP client configuration from Codex-standard paths (component reads <code>.codex/lsp-client.json</code> and <code>~/.codex/lsp-client.json</code> — see <code>components/lsp/</code> README and server-resolution modules). LazyCodex does not ship a top-level <code>lsp.toml</code>; language server mappings live in those JSON files plus env path overrides inside the LSP package.</p>
<p>The MCP registration is minimal:</p>
<pre><code class="language-json">// 161_lazycodex/plugins/omo/.mcp.json:1-8
{
  "mcpServers": {
    "lsp": {
      "command": "node",
      "args": ["./components/lsp/packages/lsp-tools-mcp/dist/cli.js", "mcp"],
      "cwd": "."
    }
  }
}
</code></pre>
<hr>
<h2>7. Telemetry component — opt-out and state dir</h2>
<p>Telemetry stores <strong>daily dedupe state only</strong> (<code>posthog-activity.json</code>), not user content:</p>
<pre><code class="language-typescript">// 161_lazycodex/plugins/omo/components/telemetry/src/posthog-activity-state.ts:16-19
const POSTHOG_ACTIVITY_STATE_FILE = "posthog-activity.json"
function getPostHogActivityStateFilePath(): string {
  return join(getActivityStateDir(), POSTHOG_ACTIVITY_STATE_FILE)
}
</code></pre>
<p>Capture logic fires at most one "active day" event per UTC day (<code>:63-80</code>). Config knobs are env-driven in <code>data-path.ts</code> (typically <code>$XDG_DATA_HOME</code> / <code>~/.local/share</code> activity dir) — operational telemetry, not product settings.</p>
<hr>
<h2>8. Ultragoal — repo-local state paths</h2>
<p>Ultragoal config is <strong>filesystem-native</strong> under <code>.omo/ultragoal/</code>:</p>
<pre><code class="language-typescript">// 161_lazycodex/plugins/omo/components/ultragoal/src/paths.ts:4-17
export function ultragoalDir(repoRoot: string): string {
  return join(repoRoot, ULTRAGOAL_DIR);
}
export function ultragoalGoalsPath(repoRoot: string): string {
  return join(ultragoalDir(repoRoot), ULTRAGOAL_GOALS);
}
export function ultragoalLedgerPath(repoRoot: string): string {
  return join(ultragoalDir(repoRoot), ULTRAGOAL_LEDGER);
}
</code></pre>
<p>These paths are relative to the <strong>git repo root</strong>, not <code>~/.codex</code> — important when classifying "config" vs "memory".</p>
<hr>
<h2>9. Hooks manifest — lifecycle wiring (not policy config)</h2>
<p><code>hooks/hooks.json</code> binds hook events to component CLIs with timeouts:</p>

3f:T6074,<h2>기초 설명</h2>
<p>MCP in LazyCodex means: Codex host reads <code>plugins/omo/.mcp.json</code>, spawns a stdio JSON-RPC process (<code>lsp-tools-mcp</code>), and routes model tool calls to LSP operations. LazyCodex does not implement discovery, auth, approval mediation, or remote SSE transports.</p>
<h2>이 문서에서 다루는 것</h2>
<ul>
<li>Architecture</li>
<li>
<ol>
<li>Aggregate manifest pointer</li>
</ol>
</li>
<li>
<ol start="2">
<li><code>.mcp.json</code> — single server registration</li>
</ol>
</li>
<li>
<ol start="3">
<li>Aggregate test — MCP isolation contract</li>
</ol>
</li>
<li>
<ol start="4">
<li>JSON-RPC server — <code>mcp.ts</code></li>
</ol>
</li>
<li>Request dispatch (<code>:49-76</code>)</li>
<li>Initialize response constants (<code>:44-46, 58-64</code>)</li>
<li>Tool call path (<code>:136-150</code>)</li>
<li>
<ol start="5">
<li>Stdio loop — idle timeout orchestration</li>
</ol>
</li>
<li>
<ol start="6">
<li>Tool registry — <code>LSP_MCP_TOOLS</code></li>
</ol>
</li>
<li>
<ol start="7">
<li>Hook ↔ MCP integration (dual path)</li>
</ol>
</li>
<li>
<ol start="8">
<li>Hooks manifest — MCP-adjacent wiring</li>
</ol>
</li>
</ul>
<h2>소스 코드 스니펫</h2>
<h3>README / docs</h3>
<pre><code class="language-mermaid">flowchart TD
  CodexHost["Codex host MCP client"] --> Manifest["plugins/omo/.mcp.json"]
  Manifest --> Spawn["node lsp-tools-mcp/dist/cli.js mcp"]
  Spawn --> Stdio["stdio JSON-RPC loop"]
  Stdio --> Methods["initialize | tools/list | tools/call"]
  Methods --> LspMgr["LSP manager + language servers"]
  LspMgr --> Tools["diagnostics | goto_definition | rename | ..."]
  PostHook["PostToolUse LSP hook"] --> Tools
</code></pre>
<h3>README / docs</h3>
<pre><code class="language-json">// 161_lazycodex/plugins/omo/.codex-plugin/plugin.json:16
"mcpServers": "./.mcp.json",
</code></pre>
<h3>README / docs</h3>
<pre><code class="language-json">// 161_lazycodex/plugins/omo/.mcp.json:1-8
{
  "mcpServers": {
    "lsp": {
      "command": "node",

      "cwd": "."
    }
  }

</code></pre>
<h3>README / docs</h3>
<pre><code class="language-javascript">// 161_lazycodex/plugins/omo/test/aggregate.test.mjs:60-70
test("#given aggregate MCP config #when inspected #then lsp server stays component isolated", async () => {
  const mcp = await readJson(".mcp.json");
  const server = mcp.mcpServers.lsp;
  assert.equal(server.command, "node");
  assert.deepEqual(server.args, ["./components/lsp/packages/lsp-tools-mcp/dist/cli.js", "mcp"]);
  assert.equal(server.cwd, ".");
});
</code></pre>
<h3>README / docs</h3>
<pre><code class="language-typescript">// 161_lazycodex/plugins/omo/components/lsp/packages/lsp-tools-mcp/src/mcp.ts:49-76
export async function handleLspMcpRequest(input: unknown): Promise&#x3C;JsonRpcResponse | undefined> {
  if (!isRecord(input)) return errorResponse(null, -32600, "Invalid Request");
  const id = jsonRpcId(input["id"]);
  const method = input["method"];
  if (method === "notifications/initialized") return undefined;
  if (method === "ping") return successResponse(id, {});
  if (method === "initialize") { /* capabilities + serverInfo */ }
  if (method === "tools/list") {
    return successResponse(id, { tools: LSP_MCP_TOOLS.map(describeTool) });
  }
  if (method === "tools/call") {
    return handleToolCall(id, input["params"]);
  }
  return errorResponse(id, -32601, `Method not found: ${String(method)}`);
}
</code></pre>
<h3>README / docs</h3>
<pre><code class="language-typescript">const SERVER_NAME = "lsp";
const SERVER_VERSION = "0.1.0";
// initialize returns:
// capabilities: { tools: { listChanged: false } }
// serverInfo: { name: SERVER_NAME, version: SERVER_VERSION }
</code></pre>
<h3>README / docs</h3>
<pre><code class="language-typescript">async function handleToolCall(id: JsonRpcId, params: unknown): Promise&#x3C;JsonRpcResponse> {
  if (!isRecord(params) || typeof params["name"] !== "string") {
    return errorResponse(id, -32602, "tools/call requires params.name");
  }
  try {
    const result = await executeLspTool(params["name"], coerceToolArguments(params["arguments"]));
    return successResponse(id, { content: result.content, isError: result.isError ?? false, details: result.details });
  } catch (error) {
    return successResponse(id, { content: [{ type: "text", text: messageFromError(error) }], isError: true });
  }
}
</code></pre>

export async function runMcpStdioServer(...) {
  const idleTimeoutMs = options.idleTimeoutMs ?? DEFAULT_IDLE_TIMEOUT_MS; // 10 * 60_000
  // ...

    const response = await handleLspMcpRequest(parsed);

<h2>코퍼스 — 009_mcp-orchestration/09_lc_mcp.md (심화)</h2>
<h1>LazyCodex MCP Orchestration</h1>
<blockquote>
<p><strong>분석 스냅샷</strong>: <code>161_lazycodex/</code> — LazyCodex exposes <strong>one</strong> MCP server (<code>lsp</code>) via the bundled <code>omo</code> Codex plugin. There is no MCP manager, OAuth broker, multi-server orchestration runtime, or web-search MCP in this repository.</p>
</blockquote>
<p>MCP in LazyCodex means: Codex host reads <code>plugins/omo/.mcp.json</code>, spawns a stdio JSON-RPC process (<code>lsp-tools-mcp</code>), and routes model tool calls to LSP operations. LazyCodex does not implement discovery, auth, approval mediation, or remote SSE transports.</p>
<h2>Architecture</h2>
<pre><code class="language-mermaid">flowchart TD
  CodexHost["Codex host MCP client"] --> Manifest["plugins/omo/.mcp.json"]
  Manifest --> Spawn["node lsp-tools-mcp/dist/cli.js mcp"]
  Spawn --> Stdio["stdio JSON-RPC loop"]
  Stdio --> Methods["initialize | tools/list | tools/call"]
  Methods --> LspMgr["LSP manager + language servers"]
  LspMgr --> Tools["diagnostics | goto_definition | rename | ..."]
  PostHook["PostToolUse LSP hook"] --> Tools
</code></pre>
<hr>
<h2>1. Aggregate manifest pointer</h2>
<p>The plugin declares MCP config location:</p>
<pre><code class="language-json">// 161_lazycodex/plugins/omo/.codex-plugin/plugin.json:16
"mcpServers": "./.mcp.json",
</code></pre>
<p>Capabilities list includes <code>"MCP Tools"</code> (<code>:23</code>) alongside Hooks and Code Intelligence — marketing metadata only; runtime is entirely in <code>.mcp.json</code> + <code>lsp-tools-mcp</code>.</p>
<hr>
<h2>2. <code>.mcp.json</code> — single server registration</h2>
<pre><code class="language-json">// 161_lazycodex/plugins/omo/.mcp.json:1-8
{
  "mcpServers": {
    "lsp": {
      "command": "node",
      "args": ["./components/lsp/packages/lsp-tools-mcp/dist/cli.js", "mcp"],
      "cwd": "."
    }
  }
}

<p><strong>Negative finding:</strong> Grep of <code>161_lazycodex/plugins/omo/.mcp.json</code> shows <strong>no</strong> <code>exa</code>, <code>tavily</code>, <code>web_search</code>, or browser MCP entries.</p>
<hr>
<h2>3. Aggregate test — MCP isolation contract</h2>
<pre><code class="language-javascript">// 161_lazycodex/plugins/omo/test/aggregate.test.mjs:60-70
test("#given aggregate MCP config #when inspected #then lsp server stays component isolated", async () => {
  const mcp = await readJson(".mcp.json");
  const server = mcp.mcpServers.lsp;
  assert.equal(server.command, "node");
  assert.deepEqual(server.args, ["./components/lsp/packages/lsp-tools-mcp/dist/cli.js", "mcp"]);
  assert.equal(server.cwd, ".");
});
</code></pre>
<p>This test encodes the <strong>orchestration boundary</strong>: MCP command paths must stay under <code>components/lsp/packages/lsp-tools-mcp/</code>, not per-component plugin ids like <code>codex-lsp@...</code> (see hooks isolation test <code>:57</code>).</p>
<hr>
<h2>4. JSON-RPC server — <code>mcp.ts</code></h2>
<h3>Request dispatch (<code>:49-76</code>)</h3>
<pre><code class="language-typescript">// 161_lazycodex/plugins/omo/components/lsp/packages/lsp-tools-mcp/src/mcp.ts:49-76
export async function handleLspMcpRequest(input: unknown): Promise&#x3C;JsonRpcResponse | undefined> {
  if (!isRecord(input)) return errorResponse(null, -32600, "Invalid Request");
  const id = jsonRpcId(input["id"]);
  const method = input["method"];
  if (method === "notifications/initialized") return undefined;
  if (method === "ping") return successResponse(id, {});
  if (method === "initialize") { /* capabilities + serverInfo */ }
  if (method === "tools/list") {
    return successResponse(id, { tools: LSP_MCP_TOOLS.map(describeTool) });
  }
  if (method === "tools/call") {
    return handleToolCall(id, input["params"]);
  }
  return errorResponse(id, -32601, `Method not found: ${String(method)}`);
}
</code></pre>
<p><strong>Supported methods:</strong></p>
<table>
<thead>
<tr>
<th>Method</th>
<th>Handler</th>
<th>Notes</th>
</tr>
</thead>
<tbody>
<tr>
<td><code>initialize</code></td>
<td><code>:58-64</code></td>
<td><code>protocolVersion</code>, <code>serverInfo.name=lsp</code>, <code>capabilities.tools</code></td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td><code>tools/list</code></td>
<td><code>:67-68</code></td>
<td>Exposes full <code>LSP_MCP_TOOLS</code> registry</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td><code>tools/call</code></td>
<td><code>:71-72</code></td>
<td>Delegates to <code>executeLspTool</code></td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td><code>ping</code></td>
<td><code>:57</code></td>
<td>Health check</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td><code>notifications/initialized</code></td>
<td><code>:56</code></td>
<td>No response (notification)</td>
</tr>
</tbody>
</table>
<p><strong>Not implemented:</strong> <code>resources/*</code>, <code>prompts/*</code>, OAuth, <code>sampling/*</code> — LSP-only subset.</p>
<h3>Initialize response constants (<code>:44-46, 58-64</code>)</h3>
<pre><code class="language-typescript">const SERVER_NAME = "lsp";

// initialize returns:
// capabilities: { tools: { listChanged: false } }
// serverInfo: { name: SERVER_NAME, version: SERVER_VERSION }

<h3>Tool call path (<code>:136-150</code>)</h3>
<pre><code class="language-typescript">async function handleToolCall(id: JsonRpcId, params: unknown): Promise&#x3C;JsonRpcResponse> {
  if (!isRecord(params) || typeof params["name"] !== "string") {
    return errorResponse(id, -32602, "tools/call requires params.name");
  }
  try {
    const result = await executeLspTool(params["name"], coerceToolArguments(params["arguments"]));
    return successResponse(id, { content: result.content, isError: result.isError ?? false, details: result.details });
  } catch (error) {
    return successResponse(id, { content: [{ type: "text", text: messageFromError(error) }], isError: true });
  }
}
</code></pre>
<p>Tool execution errors return MCP success with <code>isError: true</code> — host sees text error, not JSON-RPC fault (except malformed params).</p>
<hr>
<h2>5. Stdio loop — idle timeout orchestration</h2>
<pre><code class="language-typescript">// 161_lazycodex/plugins/omo/components/lsp/packages/lsp-tools-mcp/src/mcp.ts:78-133
export async function runMcpStdioServer(...) {
  const idleTimeoutMs = options.idleTimeoutMs ?? DEFAULT_IDLE_TIMEOUT_MS; // 10 * 60_000
  // ...
  for await (const line of lines) {
    armIdleTimer();
    const response = await handleLspMcpRequest(parsed);
    if (response) output.write(`${JSON.stringify(response)}\n`);
  }
}

<hr>
<h2>7. Hook ↔ MCP integration (dual path)</h2>
<p>Same LSP stack serves <strong>two entry points</strong>:</p>
<ol>
<li><strong>MCP tools</strong> — model-initiated via Codex MCP client</li>
<li><strong>PostToolUse hook</strong> — automatic diagnostics after edits</li>
</ol>
<pre><code class="language-typescript">// 161_lazycodex/plugins/omo/components/lsp/src/codex-hook.ts:31-63
export async function runLspPostToolUseHook(...) {
  const filePaths = extractMutatedFilePaths(input);
  // ...
  const output: PostToolUseHookOutput = {
    decision: "block",
    reason,
    hookSpecificOutput: { hookEventName: "PostToolUse", additionalContext: reason },
  };
  return `${JSON.stringify(output)}\n`;
}
</code></pre>
<p>Hook imports <code>executeLspDiagnostics</code> from <code>@code-yeongyu/lsp-tools-mcp/dist/tools.js</code> (<code>:3</code>) — <strong>shared tool implementation</strong>, different orchestration (hook JSON vs MCP JSON-RPC).</p>
<p>Mutation tools matched (<code>:27</code>): <code>apply_patch</code>, <code>write</code>, <code>edit</code>, <code>multiedit</code>, <code>multi_edit</code>.</p>
<hr>
<h2>8. Hooks manifest — MCP-adjacent wiring</h2>
<p><code>hooks/hooks.json</code> PostToolUse matcher for LSP (<code>:55-71</code>):</p>
<pre><code class="language-json">"matcher": "^(apply_patch|write|Write|edit|Edit|multi_edit|multiedit|MultiEdit)$",
"command": "node \"${PLUGIN_ROOT}/components/lsp/dist/cli.js\" hook post-tool-use",
"timeout": 60
</code></pre>
<p>60s timeout > comment-checker's 30s — LSP subprocess spawn + diagnostics aggregation can be slow on large workspaces.</p>

<hr>
<h2>11. Security notes</h2>
<ul>
<li><strong>Subprocess spawn:</strong> MCP server runs <code>node</code> with plugin-relative paths — trust boundary is Codex plugin install integrity.</li>
<li><strong>Workspace edits:</strong> <code>rename</code> tool applies LSP workspace edits — can modify many files in one MCP call (<code>tools.ts:517-523</code>).</li>
<li><strong>No URL fetch:</strong> LSP tools operate on local paths only — no SSRF surface in MCP layer (contrast web-search axis).</li>
<li><strong>Idle timeout:</strong> Server self-terminates after 10 min idle — limits orphaned language-server processes.</li>
</ul>

<h2>13. CLI entry — <code>cli.js mcp</code></h2>
<p>Spawn args from <code>.mcp.json</code> target <code>./components/lsp/packages/lsp-tools-mcp/dist/cli.js mcp</code>. The <code>mcp</code> subcommand invokes <code>runMcpStdioServer()</code> (see <code>cli.ts</code> in same package). Build prerequisite: <code>npm run build</code> in aggregate plugin workspace (<code>package.json:18</code>).</p>

  staticDedup: string[];
  dynamicDedup: Record&#x3C;string, string[]>;

<h3>README / docs</h3>
<pre><code class="language-typescript">export function hydrateEngineState(engine: Engine, cachePath: string): void {
  const state = readSessionState(cachePath);
  for (const key of state.staticDedup) engine.state.staticDedup.add(key);
  for (const [scope, keys] of Object.entries(state.dynamicDedup)) {
    engine.state.dynamicDedup.set(scope, new Set(keys));
  }
}
export function persistEngineState(engine: Engine, cachePath: string, ...): void {
  writeSessionState(cachePath, { staticDedup: [...], dynamicDedup, ... });
}
</code></pre>

  writeSessionState(cachePath, { ...emptyState(), postCompactPending: { static: true, dynamic: true } });
}
</code></pre>

export function getPostHogActivityCaptureState(now: Date = new Date()): PostHogActivityCaptureState {
  const state = readPostHogActivityState();
  const dayUTC = getUtcDayString(now);
  const captureDaily = state.lastActiveDayUTC !== dayUTC;
  if (captureDaily) writePostHogActivityState({ ...state, lastActiveDayUTC: dayUTC });
  return { dayUTC, captureDaily };
}

<h2>코퍼스 — 010_memory-pipeline/10_lc_memory.md (심화)</h2>
<h1>LazyCodex Memory Pipeline</h1>
<blockquote>
<p><strong>분석 스냅샷</strong>: <code>161_lazycodex/</code> — LazyCodex has <strong>no independent learned-memory pipeline</strong>. Memory surfaces are packaged OmO/Codex plugin components: rules session cache, ultrawork ephemeral notepad, ultragoal repo-native ledger, telemetry daily dedupe, and inherited OmO workflow docs.</p>
</blockquote>
<p>Do <strong>not</strong> classify LazyCodex as extracting facts from prior sessions, building vector indexes, or owning a replay/resume database. It packages <strong>context injection</strong>, <strong>workflow evidence</strong>, and <strong>audit ledgers</strong> — not semantic long-term memory.</p>
<h2>Architecture</h2>
<pre><code class="language-mermaid">flowchart TD
  subgraph persistent ["Persistent (disk)"]
    RulesCache["~/.codex/codex-rules/sessions/*.json"]
    Ultragoal[".omo/ultragoal/goals.json + ledger.jsonl"]
    Telemetry["posthog-activity.json (dedupe only)"]
  end
  subgraph ephemeral ["Ephemeral / session"]
    Ultrawork["/tmp/ulw-*.md notepad"]
    CodexTranscript["Codex host transcript (not LC-owned)"]
  end
  subgraph injection ["Context injection (not recall)"]
    RulesHook["rules codex-hook → additional_context"]
    UltraworkDir["ultrawork-detector.py directive"]
    UltragoalSteer["ultragoal steering hook"]
  end
  RulesCache --> RulesHook
  Ultrawork --> UltraworkDir
  Ultragoal --> UltragoalSteer
</code></pre>

<h2>2. Rules — session cache (dedupe, not semantic memory)</h2>
<h3>Cache path resolution</h3>
<pre><code class="language-typescript">// 161_lazycodex/plugins/omo/components/rules/src/persistent-cache.ts:75-77
export function sessionCachePath(sessionId: string, pluginDataRoot: string | undefined): string {
  const root = pluginDataRoot ?? process.env["PLUGIN_DATA"] ?? join(homedir(), ".codex", "codex-rules");
  return join(root, "sessions", `${safePathSegment(sessionId)}.json`);
}
</code></pre>
<p>Default root: <code>~/.codex/codex-rules/sessions/</code> unless <code>PLUGIN_DATA</code> env overrides (<code>:76</code>).</p>
<h3>Serialized state shape (<code>:14-20, 51-56</code>)</h3>
<pre><code class="language-typescript">interface SerializedSessionState {
  staticDedup: string[];
  dynamicDedup: Record&#x3C;string, string[]>;
  dynamicTargetFingerprints?: Record&#x3C;string, string>;
  postCompactPending?: PostCompactPendingState;
  compacted?: boolean;
}
</code></pre>
<p><strong>What is stored:</strong> rule injection <strong>keys already sent</strong> this session — prevents duplicate context spam. <strong>What is NOT stored:</strong> extracted user facts, embeddings, or cross-session recall.</p>
<h3>Hydrate / persist cycle (<code>:22-57</code>)</h3>
<pre><code class="language-typescript">export function hydrateEngineState(engine: Engine, cachePath: string): void {
  const state = readSessionState(cachePath);
  for (const key of state.staticDedup) engine.state.staticDedup.add(key);
  for (const [scope, keys] of Object.entries(state.dynamicDedup)) {
    engine.state.dynamicDedup.set(scope, new Set(keys));
  }
}
export function persistEngineState(engine: Engine, cachePath: string, ...): void {
  writeSessionState(cachePath, { staticDedup: [...], dynamicDedup, ... });
}
</code></pre>
<h3>Post-compact invalidation (<code>:63-73, 118-126</code>)</h3>
<p>After Codex compaction, rules hook marks pending re-injection:</p>
<pre><code class="language-typescript">export function markSessionCompacted(cachePath: string): void {
  writeSessionState(cachePath, { ...emptyState(), postCompactPending: { static: true, dynamic: true } });
}
</code></pre>
<p>Hook wiring: <code>hooks/hooks.json:85-97</code> → <code>post-compact</code> CLI resets cache with status "resetting OMO project rule cache".</p>
<h3>Rules hook events (<code>codex-hook.ts:24-69</code>)</h3>
<table>
<thead>
<tr>
<th>Event</th>
<th>Purpose</th>
</tr>
</thead>
<tbody>
<tr>
<td><code>SessionStart</code></td>
<td>Load static rules + hydrate cache</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td><code>UserPromptSubmit</code></td>
<td>Dynamic rule matching on prompt</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td><code>PostToolUse</code></td>
<td>Target fingerprint updates after <code>apply_patch</code></td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td><code>PostCompact</code></td>
<td>Mark compacted; pending reinjection</td>
</tr>
</tbody>
</table>
<p>Output format: JSON with <code>additional_context</code> for Codex host — <strong>injection</strong>, not retrieval from a memory DB.</p>
<hr>
<h2>3. Ultrawork — ephemeral notepad + directive injection</h2>
<h3>Detector hook contract</h3>
<pre><code class="language-python"># 161_lazycodex/plugins/omo/components/ultrawork/hooks/ultrawork-detector.py:1-10
"""Codex UserPromptSubmit hook: inject ultrawork directive on `ulw`/`ultrawork`.
  stdin:  JSON {cwd, hook_event_name="UserPromptSubmit", ... prompt ...}
  stdout: directive text or empty → treated as additional_context
  exit:   0 always (this hook never blocks the turn).
"""
</code></pre>
<p>Keyword match (<code>:21-22</code>):</p>
<pre><code class="language-python">ULTRAWORK_PATTERN = re.compile(r"\b(?:ultrawork|ulw)\b", re.IGNORECASE)
</code></pre>
<h3>Directive content — evidence requirements (<code>:25-45</code>)</h3>
<p>Ultrawork mode mandates:</p>
<ul>
<li>First line: <code>ULTRAWORK MODE ENABLED!</code></li>
<li>RED→GREEN test-first gate</li>
<li>Manual QA via HTTP / tmux / browser / computer-use channels</li>
<li><strong>Notepad path</strong> for evidence trail (typically <code>/tmp/ulw-*.md</code>)</li>
</ul>
<p>This is <strong>procedural memory for one task</strong>, not durable user profile memory.</p>
<h3>Bundled agents (memory-adjacent roles)</h3>
<p><code>aggregate.test.mjs:110-122</code> verifies TOMLs:</p>
<table>
<thead>
<tr>
<th>Agent</th>
<th>File</th>
<th>Memory role</th>
</tr>
</thead>
<tbody>
<tr>
<td>explorer</td>
<td><code>explorer.toml</code></td>
<td>Local codebase search — <strong>not</strong> internet</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>librarian</td>
<td><code>librarian.toml</code></td>
<td>External OSS research via host web tools</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>plan</td>
<td><code>plan.toml</code></td>
<td>Strategic planning output to <code>plans/</code></td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>codex-ultrawork-reviewer</td>
<td><code>codex-ultrawork-reviewer.toml</code></td>
<td>Verification gate</td>
</tr>
</tbody>
</table>
<p>Explorer explicitly excludes internet (<code>explorer.toml:68</code>): "External research is the librarian's job."</p>

<h2>4. Ultragoal — repo-native goal ledger</h2>
<h3>Path helpers</h3>
<pre><code class="language-typescript">// 161_lazycodex/plugins/omo/components/ultragoal/src/paths.ts:4-17
export function ultragoalDir(repoRoot: string): string {
  return join(repoRoot, ULTRAGOAL_DIR);  // .omo/ultragoal
}
export function ultragoalGoalsPath(repoRoot: string): string {
  return join(ultragoalDir(repoRoot), ULTRAGOAL_GOALS);  // goals.json
}
export function ultragoalLedgerPath(repoRoot: string): string {
  return join(ultragoalDir(repoRoot), ULTRAGOAL_LEDGER);  // ledger.jsonl
}
</code></pre>
<p><strong>Persistence model:</strong> append-only ledger + structured goals file — audit trail for multi-session <strong>objectives</strong>, not RAG memory.</p>
<h3>Steering hook</h3>
<p><code>hooks/hooks.json:45-52</code> — <code>UserPromptSubmit</code> runs ultragoal steering with 10s timeout, status "checking OMO ultragoal steering".</p>
<h3>Quality gate validation (<code>quality-gate.ts:45-70</code>)</h3>
<p>Completion requires structured evidence blocks:</p>
<pre><code class="language-typescript">export function validateQualityGate(input: unknown): UltragoalQualityGate {
  if (cleaner["status"] !== "passed") invalid(...);
  if (verification["status"] !== "passed") invalid(...);
  if (review["recommendation"] !== "APPROVE") invalid(...);
  if (review["architectStatus"] !== "CLEAR") invalid(...);
  // criteriaCoverage.passCount >= totalCriteria
}
</code></pre>
<p>This is <strong>governance memory</strong> (what evidence was accepted), not semantic recall.</p>
<hr>
<h2>5. Telemetry — dedupe state only</h2>
<pre><code class="language-typescript">// 161_lazycodex/plugins/omo/components/telemetry/src/posthog-activity-state.ts:63-80
export function getPostHogActivityCaptureState(now: Date = new Date()): PostHogActivityCaptureState {
  const state = readPostHogActivityState();
  const dayUTC = getUtcDayString(now);
  const captureDaily = state.lastActiveDayUTC !== dayUTC;
  if (captureDaily) writePostHogActivityState({ ...state, lastActiveDayUTC: dayUTC });
  return { dayUTC, captureDaily };
}
</code></pre>
<p>Stores <strong>only</strong> <code>lastActiveDayUTC</code> — no conversation content, no tool logs, no embeddings.</p>
<p>SessionStart hook (<code>hooks/hooks.json:14-22</code>) fires telemetry with 5s timeout.</p>

<h2>6. What is NOT a memory pipeline</h2>
<table>
<thead>
<tr>
<th>Feature</th>
<th>Status in LC</th>
<th>Notes</th>
</tr>
</thead>
<tbody>
<tr>
<td><code>MEMORY.md</code> / profile files</td>
<td><strong>Absent</strong></td>
<td>No grep hits in <code>161_lazycodex/</code></td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>SQLite / FTS memory index</td>
<td><strong>Absent</strong></td>
<td>Rules use JSON session files only</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>Vector embeddings</td>
<td><strong>Absent</strong></td>
<td>No embedding client in bundled components</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>Cross-session fact extraction</td>
<td><strong>Absent</strong></td>
<td>Rules cache is per-session dedupe</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>Chat replay database</td>
<td><strong>Codex host</strong></td>
<td>LC reads <code>transcript_path</code> in hooks but doesn't own store</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>Session resume DB</td>
<td><strong>Codex host</strong></td>
<td><code>SessionStart</code> input includes <code>source: resume</code> (<code>codex-hook.ts:33</code>)</td>
</tr>
</tbody>
</table>
<hr>
<h2>7. Hook transcript fields (read-only consumption)</h2>
<p>Codex hooks receive <code>transcript_path</code> in stdin JSON (<code>codex-hook.ts:28, 38, 50</code>) — path to host transcript file. Components may <strong>read</strong> for context (comment-checker <code>:49</code>) but LC source shows <strong>no writer</strong> creating a parallel memory index from transcripts.</p>

<td>Evidence notepad</td>
<td>N/A</td>
<td>ultrawork <code>/tmp/ulw-*</code></td>
<td>Devlog</td>
</tr>
</tbody>
</table>
<hr>
<h2>10. Data lifecycle diagram</h2>
<pre><code class="language-mermaid">sequenceDiagram
  participant User
  participant Codex
  participant Rules
  participant Cache as codex-rules/sessions/*.json
  participant UG as .omo/ultragoal/

  User->>Codex: prompt
  Codex->>Rules: UserPromptSubmit hook
  Rules->>Cache: hydrate + persist dedupe keys
  Rules-->>Codex: additional_context (rules text)
  Note over Cache: Cleared on PostCompact pending reinject
  User->>Codex: ultragoal checkpoint
  Codex->>UG: append ledger.jsonl
</code></pre>
<hr>
<h2>11. Security / privacy notes</h2>
<ul>
<li>Rules cache JSON may contain rule <strong>fingerprints and scope keys</strong> — not user secrets, but session-correlated (<code>safePathSegment</code> <code>:129-130</code>).</li>
<li>Ultragoal ledger is <strong>committed to repo</strong> if user commits <code>.omo/</code> — treat as team-visible audit log.</li>
<li>Telemetry: opt-out via component env (see telemetry README) — not a memory store.</li>
<li>No encryption at rest in LC components — standard filesystem permissions apply.</li>
</ul>
<hr>

<h2>코퍼스 — 011_plugin-system/11_lc_plugin.md (심화)</h2>
<h1>LazyCodex Plugin System</h1>
<blockquote>
<p><strong>분석 스냅샷</strong>: <code>161_lazycodex/</code> — LazyCodex's plugin dimension is <strong>packaging and distribution</strong>. It ships marketplace <code>sisyphuslabs</code> with a single aggregate plugin <code>omo</code> that bundles OMO Codex components under one namespace while keeping each component isolated under <code>components/</code>.</p>
</blockquote>
<p>LazyCodex does <strong>not</strong> implement OmO's full two-direction OpenCode plugin runtime. It vendored the Codex distribution surface: manifest JSON, hooks, skills sync, MCP registration, and bundled agent TOMLs.</p>
<h2>Architecture</h2>
<pre><code class="language-mermaid">flowchart TD
  Install["bunx lazycodex-ai install"] --> OmO["omo install --platform=codex"]
  OmO --> Market[".agents/plugins/marketplace.json"]
  Market --> PluginRoot["plugins/omo/"]
  PluginRoot --> Manifest[".codex-plugin/plugin.json"]
  Manifest --> Skills["skills/ (sync-skills.mjs)"]
  Manifest --> Hooks["hooks/hooks.json"]
  Manifest --> MCP[".mcp.json"]
  PluginRoot --> Components["components/* workspaces"]
  Components --> CC["comment-checker"]
  Components --> Rules["rules"]
  Components --> LSP["lsp + lsp-tools-mcp"]
  Components --> Tel["telemetry"]
  Components --> UG["ultragoal"]
  Components --> UW["ultrawork"]
</code></pre>
<hr>
<h2>1. Install path — delegation chain</h2>
<pre><code class="language-javascript">// 161_lazycodex/bin/lazycodex-ai.js:8-11
const commandArgs =
  forwardedArgs[0] === "install"
    ? ["--package", "oh-my-openagent", "omo", "install", "--platform=codex", ...forwardedArgs.slice(1)]
    : ["--package", "oh-my-openagent", "omo", ...forwardedArgs]
</code></pre>
<p>User-facing shorthand (<code>README.md:34-36</code>):</p>
<pre><code class="language-bash">bunx lazycodex-ai install
# = bunx --package oh-my-openagent omo install --platform=codex
</code></pre>
<p><strong>Plugin registration</strong> happens inside OmO installer — LC repo ships <strong>source snapshot</strong> for marketplace + aggregate plugin tree.</p>

<h2>7. Skills sync — <code>sync-skills.mjs</code></h2>
<p>Build script reference (<code>package.json:18</code>): <code>node scripts/sync-skills.mjs</code> runs before workspace builds.</p>
<p>Aggregate test (<code>aggregate.test.mjs:135-161</code>) verifies:</p>
<ul>
<li>Skills reference <code>spawn_agent(agent_type="explorer|librarian|plan")</code></li>
<li>Matching TOMLs exist at <code>components/ultrawork/agents/&#x3C;type>.toml</code></li>
</ul>
<p>This ties <strong>skill surface</strong> to <strong>bundled Codex agent roles</strong> — plugin system links skills ↔ agents.</p>
<hr>
<h2>8. Component isolation contract</h2>
<p>Test <code>#given isolated components</code> (<code>aggregate.test.mjs:38-57</code>):</p>
<pre><code class="language-javascript">const componentMarkers = [
  "components/comment-checker/dist/cli.js",
  "components/lsp/dist/cli.js",
  "components/rules/dist/cli.js",
  "components/telemetry/dist/cli.js",
  "components/ultragoal/dist/cli.js",
  "components/ultrawork/hooks/ultrawork-detector.py",
];
for (const marker of componentMarkers) {
  assert.match(text, new RegExp(marker.replaceAll("/", "\\/")));
}
assert.doesNotMatch(text, /codex-(comment-checker|lsp|rules|telemetry|ultragoal|ultrawork)@/);
</code></pre>
<p><strong>Design rule:</strong> hooks reference <strong>dist paths inside component roots</strong>, not separate marketplace plugin ids per component.</p>
<h3>Per-component plugin manifests</h3>
<p>Only <code>rules</code> declares nested <code>.codex-plugin/plugin.json</code> (<code>aggregate.test.mjs:86-107</code>):</p>
<pre><code class="language-javascript">const expectedComponentManifests = new Map([["rules", { hooks: "./hooks/hooks.json" }]]);
assert.deepEqual(componentNames, ["comment-checker", "lsp", "rules", "telemetry", "ultragoal", "ultrawork"]);
</code></pre>
<p>Other components are <strong>library packages</strong> consumed by aggregate hooks/MCP — not standalone Codex plugins in this snapshot.</p>
<hr>

<p>These agents are <strong>packaged with ultrawork component</strong> — registered via OmO installer, not listed in root <code>plugin.json</code> fields.</p>

<h2>10. Manifest ownership test</h2>
<pre><code class="language-javascript">// aggregate.test.mjs:22-36
test("#given aggregate plugin manifest #when inspected #then it owns the omo namespace", async () => {
  const manifest = await readJson(".codex-plugin/plugin.json");
  assert.equal(manifest.name, "omo");
  assert.equal(manifest.hooks, "./hooks/hooks.json");
  assert.equal(manifest.skills, "./skills/");
  assert.equal(manifest.mcpServers, "./.mcp.json");
});
</code></pre>
<hr>
<h2>11. Topology — aggregate namespace pattern</h2>
<pre><code>plugins/omo/                    ← single Codex plugin id "omo"
├── .codex-plugin/plugin.json   ← public manifest
├── hooks/hooks.json            ← fans out to components
├── .mcp.json                   ← LSP MCP only
├── skills/                     ← synced skill tree
└── components/
    ├── comment-checker/        ← PostToolUse quality
    ├── rules/                  ← context injection (+ nested manifest)
    ├── lsp/                    ← hook + lsp-tools-mcp package
    ├── telemetry/              ← SessionStart analytics
    ├── ultragoal/              ← goal steering
    └── ultrawork/              ← ulw detector + agent TOMLs
</code></pre>
<p>Each feature remains <strong>maintainable in isolation</strong> (separate workspace, tests) while <strong>exposed as one plugin</strong> to Codex host.</p>

<h2>14. Release / CI surfaces (plugin-adjacent)</h2>

<h2>코퍼스 — 012_guardian-approval/12_lc_guardian.md (심화)</h2>
<h1>LazyCodex Guardian / Approval</h1>
<blockquote>
<p><strong>분석 스냅샷</strong>: <code>161_lazycodex/</code> — LazyCodex has <strong>no independent guardian/approval subsystem</strong>. It is a wrapper + plugin bundle. Execution approval (file/shell/MCP) remains <strong>Codex host-owned</strong>. LC-local evidence shows post-edit quality blockers, ultrawork reviewer gates, and ultragoal completion governance.</p>
</blockquote>
<p>Distinguish three layers: (1) <strong>host permission</strong> before tool runs, (2) <strong>PostToolUse block</strong> after edits fail quality checks, (3) <strong>workflow verdict</strong> agents (reviewer / quality gate) that govern "done" — not sandbox policy.</p>
<h2>Architecture</h2>
<pre><code class="language-mermaid">flowchart TD
  subgraph host ["Codex host (not LC code)"]
    PreApprove["file/shell/MCP approval"]
    Sandbox["sandbox policy"]
  end
  subgraph lc_hooks ["LC PostToolUse hooks"]
    CC["comment-checker → decision:block"]
    LSP["lsp diagnostics → decision:block"]
  end
  subgraph workflow ["LC workflow gates"]
    Reviewer["codex-ultrawork-reviewer TOML"]
    QG["ultragoal quality-gate.ts"]
  end
  ToolRun["apply_patch / write / edit"] --> PreApprove
  PreApprove --> ToolRun
  ToolRun --> CC
  ToolRun --> LSP
  CC --> BlockTurn["Hook block → user/model sees reason"]
  LSP --> BlockTurn
  UltraworkDone["ulw completion claim"] --> Reviewer
  GoalDone["ultragoal checkpoint"] --> QG
</code></pre>
<hr>
<h2>1. Gate type taxonomy</h2>
<table>
<thead>
<tr>
<th>Gate</th>
<th>Type</th>
<th>Owner</th>
<th>Behavior</th>
</tr>
</thead>
<tbody>
<tr>
<td>Codex file/shell/MCP approval</td>
<td>Pre-tool</td>
<td><strong>Codex host</strong></td>
<td>Permission modes in hook stdin (<code>permission_mode</code> field)</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>Comment checker</td>
<td>Post-tool quality</td>
<td>LC component</td>
<td><code>decision: "block"</code> on warnings (<code>codex-hook.ts:62-65</code>)</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>LSP diagnostics</td>
<td>Post-tool quality</td>
<td>LC component</td>
<td><code>decision: "block"</code> on errors (<code>codex-hook.ts:55-63</code>)</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>Ultrawork reviewer</td>
<td>Workflow verdict</td>
<td>Bundled agent TOML</td>
<td>APPROVE vs REJECTION strings</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>Ultragoal quality gate</td>
<td>Completion governance</td>
<td><code>quality-gate.ts</code></td>
<td>Structured evidence schema</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>Rules</td>
<td>Context policy</td>
<td>LC component</td>
<td>Injects instructions — <strong>not</strong> permission decisions</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>Ultrawork detector</td>
<td>Context injection</td>
<td>Python hook</td>
<td><code>exit: 0 always</code> — never blocks (<code>ultrawork-detector.py:10</code>)</td>
</tr>
</tbody>
</table>
<hr>
<h2>2. Hooks manifest — no PreToolUse / PermissionRequest</h2>
<pre><code class="language-json">// 161_lazycodex/plugins/omo/hooks/hooks.json — events present:
// SessionStart, UserPromptSubmit, PostToolUse, PostCompact
// ABSENT: PreToolUse, PermissionRequest, SubagentStop
</code></pre>
<p>Grep of full <code>hooks.json</code> (99 lines) confirms LC bundle does <strong>not</strong> register pre-execution permission hooks — those would be host-native or OmO OpenCode paths.</p>
<p>Hook stdin always includes <code>permission_mode</code> (e.g. <code>codex-hook.ts:21, 43, 54</code>) — <strong>read-only consumption</strong> of host state, not evaluation.</p>
<hr>
<h2>3. Comment checker — PostToolUse block</h2>
<h3>Block output shape</h3>
<pre><code class="language-typescript">// 161_lazycodex/plugins/omo/components/comment-checker/src/codex-hook.ts:60-65
if (warnings.length === 0) return "";

return JSON.stringify({
  decision: "block",
  reason: formatWarnings(warnings),
});
</code></pre>
<h3>Processing loop (<code>:35-58</code>)</h3>
<pre><code class="language-typescript">export async function runCommentCheckerPostToolUse(input: CodexPostToolUseInput, ...): Promise&#x3C;string> {
  const requests = extractCodexCommentCheckRequests(input);
  if (requests.length === 0) return "";
  for (const request of requests) {
    const result = await runner(toHookInput(request, context));
    if (result.status === "missing" || result.status === "pass") continue;
    if (result.status === "error") continue;
    // accumulate warnings
  }
}
</code></pre>
<table>
<thead>
<tr>
<th>Result status</th>
<th>Hook effect</th>
</tr>
</thead>
<tbody>
<tr>
<td><code>missing</code> / <code>pass</code></td>
<td>No block</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td><code>error</code></td>
<td>Silent continue (no block)</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>warning message</td>
<td>Contributes to <code>decision: block</code></td>
</tr>
</tbody>
</table>
<p>Hook wiring: <code>hooks/hooks.json:59-64</code> — 30s timeout, matcher on edit tools.</p>
<hr>
<h2>4. LSP diagnostics — PostToolUse block</h2>

  decision: "block";
  reason: string;
  hookSpecificOutput: {
    hookEventName: "PostToolUse";
    additionalContext: string;
  };
}

<h3>Mutation tool detection (<code>:27, 66-96</code>)</h3>

<h3>Clean diagnostic bypass (<code>:98-100</code>)</h3>
<pre><code class="language-typescript">function isCleanDiagnostics(diagnostics: string): boolean {
  return diagnostics.length === 0 || diagnostics.includes(CLEAN_DIAGNOSTICS_TEXT) || ...
}
</code></pre>
<p>Only <strong>error-severity</strong> diagnostics fetched (<code>:32</code> — <code>severity: "error"</code> in <code>runLspDiagnosticsText</code>).</p>
<p>Hook timeout: <strong>60s</strong> (<code>hooks/hooks.json:67-69</code>) — longest PostToolUse hook.</p>
<hr>
<h2>5. Ultrawork reviewer — workflow approval agent</h2>
<pre><code class="language-toml"># 161_lazycodex/plugins/omo/components/ultrawork/agents/codex-ultrawork-reviewer.toml:1-17
name = "codex-ultrawork-reviewer"
description = "Strict ultrawork verification reviewer..."
model = "gpt-5.2"
model_reasoning_effort = "xhigh"
</code></pre>
<p>Verdict rules (<code>developer_instructions</code>):</p>
<ul>
<li><code>UNCONDITIONAL APPROVAL</code> — all criteria + real-surface evidence</li>
<li><code>REJECTION</code> — missing evidence, avoidable risk, scope drift</li>
<li>"looks good but..." treated as <strong>rejection</strong></li>
</ul>
<p>This is <strong>LLM-as-judge</strong>, not deterministic policy engine — orchestrated by ultrawork workflow/skills, not <code>hooks.json</code>.</p>
<hr>
<h2>6. Ultragoal quality gate — completion governance</h2>
<pre><code class="language-typescript">// 161_lazycodex/plugins/omo/components/ultragoal/src/quality-gate.ts:45-58
export function validateQualityGate(input: unknown): UltragoalQualityGate {
  if (cleaner["status"] !== "passed") invalid("aiSlopCleaner.status must be passed.", ...);
  if (verification["status"] !== "passed") invalid("verification.status must be passed.", ...);
  if (review["recommendation"] !== "APPROVE") invalid("recommendation must be APPROVE.", ...);
  if (review["architectStatus"] !== "CLEAR") invalid("architectStatus must be CLEAR.", ...);
  const totalCriteria = numberField(coverage["totalCriteria"], ...);
  const passCount = numberField(coverage["passCount"], ...);
  if (passCount &#x3C; totalCriteria) invalid("criteriaCoverage.passCount must cover totalCriteria.", ...);
}
</code></pre>
<p>Required sections:</p>
<table>
<thead>
<tr>
<th>Section</th>
<th>Required state</th>
</tr>
</thead>
<tbody>
<tr>
<td><code>aiSlopCleaner</code></td>
<td><code>status: "passed"</code> + evidence</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td><code>verification</code></td>
<td><code>status: "passed"</code> + commands[] + evidence</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td><code>codeReview</code></td>
<td><code>recommendation: "APPROVE"</code>, <code>architectStatus: "CLEAR"</code></td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td><code>criteriaCoverage</code></td>
<td><code>passCount >= totalCriteria</code></td>
</tr>
</tbody>
</table>
<p>Blocker classification helpers (<code>:73-80</code>) normalize external auth failures (GHCR 401/403 patterns) — <strong>governance</strong>, not tool permission.</p>
<p>Steering hook: <code>hooks/hooks.json:45-52</code> — ultragoal <code>user-prompt-submit</code> (injection/steering, not block).</p>
<hr>
<h2>7. Rules — context injection (not guardian)</h2>
<p>Rules hooks return <code>additional_context</code> JSON — they <strong>add</strong> instructions when matches fire. No <code>decision: "block"</code> in rules <code>codex-hook.ts</code> for standard paths.</p>
<p>PostCompact resets cache (<code>hooks/hooks.json:85-97</code>) — session hygiene, not approval.</p>
<p>Env master switch: <code>CODEX_RULES_DISABLED</code> (<code>config.ts:8</code>) disables rules entirely — soft off, not security boundary.</p>
<hr>
<h2>8. Ultrawork detector — non-blocking</h2>
<pre><code class="language-python"># ultrawork-detector.py:10
# exit: 0 always (this hook never blocks the turn).
</code></pre>
<p>Injects large <code>&#x3C;ultrawork-mode></code> directive on <code>ulw</code>/<code>ultrawork</code> keywords — <strong>raises bar</strong> via prompt, not hook block.</p>
<hr>
<h2>9. CLI wrapper — no approval logic</h2>
<pre><code class="language-javascript">// 161_lazycodex/bin/lazycodex-ai.js — entire file is spawnSync forwarding
// No permission evaluation, no risk scoring, no ask/deny engine
</code></pre>
<hr>
<h2>10. Comparison — post-tool block vs host guardian</h2>
<table>
<thead>
<tr>
<th>Aspect</th>
<th>Codex host guardian</th>
<th>LC PostToolUse hooks</th>
</tr>
</thead>
<tbody>
<tr>
<td>Timing</td>
<td>Before/during tool execution</td>
<td>After successful edit tools</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>Scope</td>
<td>All tools (shell, MCP, etc.)</td>
<td>Matcher-limited edit tools</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>Mechanism</td>
<td>Policy engine / TUI</td>
<td>JSON <code>decision: "block"</code></td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>Reversible</td>
<td>User approves/denies</td>
<td>Model must fix and retry</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>Config</td>
<td><code>config.toml</code>, MDM</td>
<td>Hook subprocess timeouts</td>
</tr>
</tbody>
</table>
<p>LC hooks are <strong>quality gates</strong>, not replacement for host sandbox.</p>
<hr>
<h2>11. Parity matrix — guardian axis</h2>
<table>

<tr>
<th>Concern</th>

<hr>
<h2>12. Security notes</h2>
<ul>
<li>PostToolUse blocks run <strong>after</strong> patch applied — race: bad code briefly on disk before block surfaces to model.</li>
<li>Comment checker <code>error</code> status does not block (<code>codex-hook.ts:53</code>) — silent pass on checker failures.</li>
<li>LSP hook skips failed tool responses (<code>codex-hook.ts:68</code>) — no double-penalty on failed edits.</li>
<li>Reviewer agent is prompt-based — no cryptographic attestation of evidence.</li>
<li>No allowlist/denylist for URLs or paths in LC guardian layer (contrast web-search SSRF — host concern).</li>
</ul>
<hr>
<h2>13. Operational workflow (ultrawork + gates)</h2>
<ol>
<li>User prompts with <code>ulw</code> → detector injects ultrawork directive (non-blocking)</li>
<li>Model edits files → host may approve tools per <code>permission_mode</code></li>
<li>PostToolUse → comment-checker + LSP may <code>block</code> with reasons</li>
<li>Model fixes issues → loops until hooks pass</li>
<li>Before "done" → spawn <code>codex-ultrawork-reviewer</code> for verdict</li>
<li>Ultragoal checkpoints → <code>validateQualityGate</code> on structured JSON evidence</li>
</ol>
<hr>

<h2>코퍼스 — 013_etc/13_lc_etc.md (심화)</h2>
<h1>LazyCodex Residual / Cross-Cutting Notes</h1>
<blockquote>
<p><strong>분석 스냅샷</strong>: <code>161_lazycodex/</code> — LazyCodex's residual surface is <strong>product packaging</strong>, documentation, release infrastructure, and marketing around OmO/Codex distribution. This axis captures cross-cutting concerns that do not map cleanly to config/MCP/memory/plugin/guardian/web-search.</p>
</blockquote>
<p>LazyCodex is intentionally thin: a CLI shim (<code>bin/lazycodex-ai.js</code>), marketplace snapshot, bundled <code>plugins/omo</code> aggregate plugin, and <code>packages/web</code> docs site. Heavy harness logic lives in <strong>delegated</strong> <code>oh-my-openagent</code> (OmO).</p>
<h2>Architecture — repository layout</h2>
<pre><code class="language-mermaid">flowchart LR
  Root["161_lazycodex/"]

  Root --> Agents[".agents/plugins/marketplace.json"]
  Root --> Plugin["plugins/omo/"]
  Root --> Web["packages/web/"]
  Root --> GH[".github/workflows/"]
  Root --> Readme["README.md"]
  Plugin --> Comp["components/*"]
  Web --> Docs["content/docs/"]
</code></pre>

<h2>1. Product positioning vs implementation evidence</h2>
<p>README headline (<code>README.md:6-7, 60-64</code>):</p>
<blockquote>
<p><strong>Codex for no-brainers.</strong> LazyCodex wraps OmO so you don't have to think about setup. Think LazyVim for lazy.nvim, but for Codex.</p>
</blockquote>
<p>Feature table (<code>:68-77</code>):</p>

<th>README claim</th>

</tr>
<tr>

<td>Multiple agents on subtasks</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>Multi-Model Routing</td>
<td>Automatic model selection</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>Skills System</td>
<td>Extensible skill library</td>
</tr>

<td>Sensible defaults</td>
</tr>
</tbody>
</table>
<p><strong>Implementation split:</strong> README describes <strong>OmO capabilities</strong>; LC repo evidence is primarily wrapper + <code>plugins/omo</code> bundle + docs — not full OmO source tree.</p>

<h2>4. Website — <code>packages/web</code></h2>
<p>Docs/marketing site (Next.js stack per README architecture section):</p>

<p>Web package does not implement agent harness, hooks, or MCP — pure product surface.</p>

</tr>
</tbody>
</table>
<p>CI validates that hook paths like <code>components/*/dist/cli.js</code> exist post-build — ties release pipeline to <strong>plugin artifact integrity</strong> (<code>aggregate.test.mjs</code> isolation tests).</p>
<hr>
<h2>6. Component packaging summary</h2>
<p>Aggregate plugin workspaces (<code>plugins/omo/package.json:8-16</code>):</p>
<pre><code>comment-checker, rules, lsp, lsp-tools-mcp, telemetry, ultragoal, ultrawork
</code></pre>
<p>Build pipeline (<code>:18</code>):</p>
<pre><code>sync-skills.mjs → sync-telemetry-component.mjs → npm run build --workspaces
</code></pre>
<p>Each component maintains isolated README under <code>components/&#x3C;name>/README.md</code> — telemetry README documents PostHog boundaries and opt-out env vars.</p>
<hr>
<h2>7. Telemetry — cross-cutting operational concern</h2>
<p>PostHog daily-active capture (<code>telemetry/src/posthog-activity-state.ts:63-80</code>):</p>
<ul>
<li>Fires on SessionStart hook (<code>hooks/hooks.json:14-22</code>)</li>
<li>Stores only <code>lastActiveDayUTC</code> in <code>posthog-activity.json</code></li>
<li>Not user content logging — operational analytics with dedupe</li>
</ul>
<p>Cross-ref: <code>008_lc_config.md</code> telemetry section, <code>010_lc_memory.md</code> (explicitly not memory).</p>

<h2>15. Release artifacts</h2>
<p>Typical publish surfaces:</p>
<ul>
<li>npm package exposing <code>bin/lazycodex-ai.js</code></li>
<li>GitHub releases (workflows)</li>
<li>lazycodex.ai docs deploy</li>
</ul>
<p>Version in aggregate plugin: <code>0.1.0</code> (<code>plugin.json:3</code>) — may lag OmO semver; track on sync.</p>
<hr>
<h2>15.1 npm package surface</h2>
<p>The published <code>lazycodex-ai</code> npm package exposes only the wrapper binary — not the full <code>plugins/omo</code> tree as runtime dependency. Users who <code>bunx lazycodex-ai install</code> pull OmO which registers the vendored plugin snapshot from OmO's install path, not by compiling LC repo locally.</p>
<p>Local developers working in <code>161_lazycodex/</code> run aggregate plugin tests via:</p>
<pre><code class="language-bash">cd plugins/omo &#x26;&#x26; npm run check
# package.json:19 — "check": "npm run build &#x26;&#x26; npm test"
</code></pre>
<p>This validates dist paths referenced in <code>hooks/hooks.json</code> before release.</p>
<hr>
<h2>15.2 License and attribution chain</h2>
<p>Aggregate plugin declares MIT (<code>plugin.json:12</code>). Component workspaces inherit upstream OmO licensing. LC repo is a <strong>distribution fork snapshot</strong> — legal/provenance tracking belongs in release notes when syncing from <code>172_oh-my-openagent</code>.</p>
<p>Author metadata (<code>plugin.json:5-8</code>):</p>
<pre><code class="language-json">"author": {
  "name": "Yeongyu Kim",
  "email": "yeongyu@users.noreply.github.com",
  "url": "https://github.com/code-yeongyu"
}
</code></pre>
<p>Repository links point to <code>code-yeongyu/omo</code> — LC is branded separately (LazyCodex / Sisyphus Labs marketplace) but shares authorship lineage.</p>
<hr>
<h2>15.3 <code>packages/web</code> command strings</h2>
<p>Site config centralizes install copy so docs and landing page stay aligned with shim behavior. When README drift is fixed upstream, update <strong>both</strong> <code>README.md</code> and <code>packages/web/lib/site-config.ts</code> — corpus treats shim + marketplace as runtime truth, web as user-facing mirror.</p>
<p>Docs paths under <code>packages/web/content/docs/</code> include overview, install, ultrawork, start-work — each describes OmO workflows re-exported through LazyCodex branding.</p>
<hr>
<h2>15.4 Submodule vs plugin snapshot maintenance</h2>
<p>When <code>src/</code> git submodule is initialized, it may contain a newer OmO harness than <code>plugins/omo</code> snapshot. Release maintainers sync:</p>
<ol>
<li>OmO upstream changes</li>
<li><code>plugins/omo</code> component copies</li>
<li><code>sync-skills.mjs</code> + <code>sync-telemetry-component.mjs</code></li>
<li><code>aggregate.test.mjs</code> green</li>
</ol>
<p>Corpus readers: if submodule and <code>plugins/omo</code> diverge, <strong>prefer <code>plugins/omo</code> paths</strong> for Codex plugin axis citations unless analyzing full OmO harness features explicitly.</p>

<h2>코퍼스 — 014_web-search/14_lc_web-search.md (심화)</h2>
<h1>LazyCodex Web Search / Research</h1>
<blockquote>
<p><strong>분석 스냅샷</strong>: <code>161_lazycodex/</code> — LazyCodex does <strong>not</strong> own a general web-search engine, browser runtime, or first-party web-search MCP server. Web/search is <strong>host-mediated</strong>: Codex host tools (<code>web_search</code>, <code>webfetch</code>) invoked per bundled <strong>librarian</strong> agent instructions in <code>librarian.toml</code>.</p>
</blockquote>
<p>The only MCP server in LC is <strong>LSP</strong> (<code>.mcp.json</code>) — local symbol/diagnostic tools, not internet search.</p>
<h2>Architecture</h2>
<pre><code class="language-mermaid">flowchart TD
  User["User question about external library"] --> Orchestrator["OmO ultrawork / spawn_agent"]
  Orchestrator --> Librarian["librarian.toml agent"]
  Librarian --> HostSearch["Codex host web_search"]
  Librarian --> HostFetch["Codex host webfetch"]
  Librarian --> GhCLI["gh search / gh api / clone"]
  HostSearch --> Internet["Public web"]
  HostFetch --> Internet
  GhCLI --> GitHub["GitHub API + repos"]
  LSPMCP["LSP MCP symbols"] --> LocalCode["Local workspace only"]
  LSPMCP -.->|"NOT web search"| X["❌"]
</code></pre>
