<hr>
<h2>2. CLI — no search commands</h2>
<pre><code class="language-javascript">// 161_lazycodex/bin/lazycodex-ai.js:8-11
const commandArgs =
  forwardedArgs[0] === "install"
    ? ["--package", "oh-my-openagent", "omo", "install", "--platform=codex", ...]
    : ["--package", "oh-my-openagent", "omo", ...forwardedArgs]
</code></pre>
<p>Grep of entire <code>161_lazycodex/bin/</code> — no <code>/web</code>, <code>search</code>, <code>scrape</code>, or URL fetch implementation.</p>
<p>Contrast Aider <code>/web</code> slash command — see <code>14_ai_web-search.md</code>.</p>
<hr>
<h2>3. MCP boundary — LSP only</h2>
<pre><code class="language-json">// 161_lazycodex/plugins/omo/.mcp.json:1-8
{
  "mcpServers": {
    "lsp": {
      "command": "node",
      "args": ["./components/lsp/packages/lsp-tools-mcp/dist/cli.js", "mcp"],
      "cwd": "."
    }
  }
}
</code></pre>
<p>Aggregate test locks this contract (<code>aggregate.test.mjs:60-70</code>).</p>
<h3>LSP symbols ≠ web search</h3>
<pre><code class="language-typescript">// 161_lazycodex/plugins/omo/components/lsp/packages/lsp-tools-mcp/src/tools.ts:619-636
{
  name: "symbols",
  aliases: ["lsp_symbols"],
  description: "List document symbols or search workspace symbols.",
  inputSchema: objectSchema({
    filePath: { type: "string", ... },
    scope: { enum: ["document", "workspace"], ... },
    query: { type: "string", description: "Workspace symbol query." },
  }, ["filePath", "scope"]),
}
</code></pre>
<p><code>workspace</code> scope queries <strong>LSP workspace symbols</strong> — indexed source in repo, not Google/Bing.</p>
<hr>
<h2>4. Librarian agent — host tool orchestration</h2>
<h3>Agent metadata</h3>
<pre><code class="language-toml"># 161_lazycodex/plugins/omo/components/ultrawork/agents/librarian.toml:1-6
name = "librarian"
description = "External open-source codebase and documentation researcher..."
model = "gpt-5.4-mini"
model_reasoning_effort = "low"
service_tier = "fast"
</code></pre>
<p>Read-only mandate (<code>:207-208</code>):</p>
<blockquote>
<p>Tools I will NEVER call: <code>edit</code>, <code>write</code>, <code>apply_patch</code> ... Cloning into <code>${TMPDIR:-/tmp}</code> is allowed; cloning into the working tree is not.</p>
</blockquote>
<h3>Phase 0.5 — documentation discovery (web_search + webfetch)</h3>
<pre><code class="language-toml"># librarian.toml:42-58 (representative)
## Step 1 - find official documentation
- `web_search("&#x3C;library-name> official documentation")` -> pick the official URL
## Step 2 - version check
- `web_search("&#x3C;library-name> v&#x3C;version> documentation")`
## Step 3 - sitemap discovery
- `webfetch(&#x3C;base>/sitemap.xml)`. Fallbacks: `/sitemap-0.xml`, ...
## Step 4 - targeted investigation
- `webfetch(&#x3C;specific-doc-page-from-sitemap>)`
</code></pre>
<p><strong>Critical:</strong> <code>web_search</code> and <code>webfetch</code> appear as <strong>tool names in agent instructions</strong> — not implemented in LC repo. Availability depends on <strong>Codex host tool registry</strong> at runtime.</p>
<h3>Date awareness (<code>:19-23</code>)</h3>
<pre><code class="language-toml"># CRITICAL: DATE AWARENESS
Before any search, check the current date from the environment.
- NEVER query with last year's date.
- ALWAYS include the current year in time-sensitive queries
</code></pre>
<p>Prompt engineering for search quality — not LC code.</p>
<h3>Tool reference section (<code>:143-155</code>)</h3>
<table>
<thead>
<tr>
<th>Purpose</th>
<th>Instructed tool</th>
</tr>
</thead>
<tbody>
<tr>
<td>Official docs discovery</td>
<td><code>web_search("library official documentation")</code></td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>Versioned docs</td>
<td><code>web_search</code> + <code>webfetch(/versions)</code></td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>Sitemap</td>
<td><code>webfetch(sitemap.xml)</code></td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>Read page</td>
<td><code>webfetch(url)</code></td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>Latest info</td>
<td><code>web_search("&#x3C;query> &#x3C;CURRENT_YEAR>")</code></td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>Code search</td>
<td><code>gh search code</code></td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>Issues/PRs</td>
<td>`gh search issues</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>Clone</td>
<td><code>gh repo clone ... --depth 1</code></td>
</tr>
</tbody>
</table>
<p>GitHub CLI tools are <strong>local subprocess tools</strong> (when <code>gh</code> installed) — distinct from hosted <code>web_search</code>.</p>
<hr>
<h2>5. Explorer — explicit non-web boundary</h2>
<pre><code class="language-toml"># 161_lazycodex/plugins/omo/components/ultrawork/agents/explorer.toml:68
- Do not browse the internet. External research is the librarian's job.
</code></pre>
<p>Role separation prevents duplicate web traffic and confines local repo search to explorer.</p>
<hr>
<h2>6. Request type taxonomy (librarian)</h2>
<p>From <code>librarian.toml:27-34</code>:</p>
<table>
<thead>
<tr>
<th>Type</th>
<th>Pattern</th>
<th>Primary tools</th>
</tr>
</thead>
<tbody>
<tr>
<td>TYPE A — CONCEPTUAL</td>
<td>"How do I use X?"</td>
<td>Phase 0.5 docs + web_search + webfetch</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>TYPE B — IMPLEMENTATION</td>
<td>"Show me source of Z"</td>
<td>gh clone + rg + permalinks</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>TYPE C — CONTEXT/HISTORY</td>
<td>"Why was X changed?"</td>
<td>gh issues/PRs + git log/blame</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>TYPE D — COMPREHENSIVE</td>
<td>Complex/ambiguous</td>
<td>Phase 0.5 + parallel 6+ calls</td>
</tr>
</tbody>
</table>
<p>Parallel requirements table (<code>:167-172</code>) — orchestration guidance in TOML, not LC scheduler code.</p>
<hr>
<h2>7. Citation contract — evidence output format</h2>
<p>Mandatory permalink format (<code>:128-139</code>):</p>
<pre><code class="language-text">https://github.com/&#x3C;owner>/&#x3C;repo>/blob/&#x3C;commit-sha>/&#x3C;filepath>#L&#x3C;start>-L&#x3C;end>
</code></pre>
<p>Never link to branch names (<code>/blob/main/...</code>) — SHA-pinned for verifiability.</p>
<p>This shapes <strong>search output quality</strong> — librarian returns citations, not raw search dumps.</p>
<hr>
<h2>8. Failure recovery (search paths)</h2>
<p>From <code>librarian.toml:192-201</code>:</p>
<table>
<thead>
<tr>
<th>Failure</th>
<th>Recovery</th>
</tr>
</thead>
<tbody>
<tr>
<td>Docs indexer empty</td>
<td>Clone repo, read source + README</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td><code>gh search code</code> empty</td>
<td>Broaden query, search forks</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>gh API rate-limited</td>
<td>Use cloned repo in <code>${TMPDIR}</code></td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>Sitemap missing</td>
<td>Fallback XML paths or parse nav</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>Sources disagree</td>
<td>Surface disagreement — no guessing</td>
</tr>
</tbody>
</table>
<p>LC does not implement retry logic — agent prompt policy only.</p>
<hr>
<h2>9. Skills ↔ librarian linkage</h2>
<pre><code class="language-javascript">// aggregate.test.mjs:135-161
// Skills with spawn_agent(agent_type="librarian") must have matching TOML
assert.deepEqual(expected, ["explorer", "librarian", "plan"]);
const tomlPath = join(root, "components", "ultrawork", "agents", `${agentType}.toml`);
</code></pre>
<p>Web research is <strong>skill-orchestrated</strong> via agent spawn — not user slash command in LC.</p>

<p><code>plugins/omo/README.md</code> lists components (comment-checker, rules, lsp, telemetry, ultragoal, ultrawork) — <strong>no web-search component</strong> directory.</p>
<p>Plugin capabilities (<code>plugin.json:23</code>) include "Code Intelligence" (LSP) and "Workflow" (ultrawork) — not "Web Search".</p>

<h2>13. Host dependency checklist</h2>
<p>After Codex upgrade, re-verify:</p>
<ol>
<li>Host exposes <code>web_search</code> tool to models using librarian</li>
<li>Host exposes <code>webfetch</code> with acceptable size/SSRF policy</li>
<li><code>gh</code> CLI available on PATH for GitHub research paths</li>
<li>Librarian model id in TOML still valid (<code>gpt-5.4-mini</code> at <code>:4</code>)</li>
</ol>
<p>LC manifest does <strong>not</strong> gate or configure host search — zero lines in <code>lazycodex-ai.js</code> or <code>.mcp.json</code>.</p>
<hr>
<h2>14. Security notes</h2>
<ul>
<li><strong>SSRF:</strong> Any URL librarian passes to <code>webfetch</code> is fetched by <strong>host</strong> — LC has no domain allowlist.</li>
<li><strong>Read-only librarian:</strong> Cannot <code>write</code>/<code>apply_patch</code> — reduces exfil-via-edit risk; still can clone public repos to <code>/tmp</code>.</li>
<li><strong>Secrets in URLs:</strong> Prompt says short quotes only (<code>:210</code>) — no LC enforcement code.</li>
<li><strong>LSP MCP:</strong> Local paths only — no network in MCP layer.</li>
</ul>
<hr>
<h2>15. Comparison with LSP MCP search confusion</h2>
<p>Operators sometimes conflate:</p>
<table>
<thead>
<tr>
<th>Tool</th>
<th>Scope</th>
<th>Network</th>
</tr>
</thead>
<tbody>
<tr>
<td><code>lsp_symbols</code> query</td>
<td>Workspace AST/index</td>
<td>No</td>
</tr>

<td>Public internet</td>
<td>Yes (host)</td>
</tr>

<h2>16. Web package — docs only</h2>
<p><code>packages/web/content/docs/overview.md</code> frames LazyCodex as distribution layer — marketing copy, not search backend.</p>

<hr>
<h2>17. Operational workflow (librarian path)</h2>
<ol>
<li>Orchestrator spawns librarian for external-library question</li>
<li>Librarian classifies request TYPE A–D (<code>librarian.toml:27-34</code>)</li>
<li>Phase 0.5: <code>web_search</code> → official docs URL → <code>webfetch</code> sitemap → targeted pages</li>
<li>Parallel: <code>gh search code</code>, optional shallow clone, issues/PRs</li>
<li>Synthesis: SHA-pinned markdown citations (<code>:109-126</code>)</li>
<li>Explorer handles local repo if question is in working tree — not librarian</li>
</ol>

<h2>소스 코드 스니펫</h2>
<h3><code>161_lazycodex/README.md</code></h3>
<h2>🚀 Install</h2>
<p>One line. No global install, no <code>npm i -g</code>. Always use <code>bunx</code>:</p>
<pre><code class="language-bash">bunx lazycodex-ai install
</code></pre>
<p>This is shorthand for <code>bunx --package oh-my-openagent omo install --platform=codex</code>. For a fully autonomous, no-TUI setup:</p>
<pre><code class="language-bash">bunx lazycodex-ai install --no-tui --codex-autonomous
</code></pre>
<h2>코퍼스 — 015_reverse-engineering/ (심화)</h2>
<h3><code>015_reverse-engineering/00_reverse_evidence_policy.md</code></h3>
<h1>Reverse Engineering Evidence Policy</h1>
<p>이 축은 설치 help parity 문서의 다음 단계다. 기존 <code>00</code>~<code>14</code> 축은 주로 help/config/local-doc 표면을 비교했고, 이 축은 설치된 바이너리와 번들에서 복원 가능한 구조를 따로 기록한다.</p>
<h2>Evidence Levels</h2>
<table>
<thead>
<tr>
<th>Level</th>
<th>의미</th>
<th>사용할 수 있는 주장</th>
</tr>
</thead>
<tbody>
<tr>
<td>installed-help</td>
<td><code>--help</code>, public command output, version output</td>
<td>명령/플래그/공개 subcommand가 존재한다</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>safe-local-doc</td>
<td>설치 패키지의 docs, changelog, examples, manifest</td>
<td>문서화된 schema/경로/기능 설명이 있다</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>bundle-key</td>
<td>minified bundle에 남은 module key, source path, route name, proto name</td>
<td>내부 모듈/라우터/프로토/컴포넌트가 존재한다</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>binary-string</td>
<td>native binary <code>strings</code>, <code>file</code>, <code>otool</code>, <code>codesign</code>, <code>nm</code></td>
<td>crate/package/protocol/tool/evaluator 이름이 embedded되어 있다</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>runtime-trace</td>
<td>synthetic project에서 실제 명령을 실행한 결과</td>
<td>동작 semantics, precedence, permission enforcement를 확인했다</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>private-artifact-name</td>
<td>비공개 상태 파일의 경로/개수만 관찰</td>
<td>artifact가 존재한다. 내용/schema 주장은 금지</td>
</tr>
</tbody>
</table>
<p><code>/Users/jun/Developer/codex/015_reverse-engineering/33_source_deobfuscation_inventory.md</code> further separates source-like recovery levels. In this corpus, Cursor reaches preserved module-key recovery, while Grok/Kiro/AGY mostly expose native source-path, handler, protobuf, and runtime-trace evidence. Do not call this "full source recovered" unless a real source map or readable source archive is present.</p>
<h2>Hard Boundary</h2>
<p>역분석의 목적은 제품 구조 복원이지 사용자 상태 추출이 아니다. 다음은 내용 읽기 금지다.</p>
<ul>
<li>auth/token/cookie/credential/login data</li>
<li>raw transcript, chat history, conversation DB/PB</li>
<li>logs and terminal captures</li>
<li>browser profile state, local storage, IndexedDB, session storage</li>
<li>memory/goal runtime stores</li>
<li>screenshots and browser recordings</li>
<li>private <code>mcp.json</code>, settings, config values unless explicitly redacted</li>
</ul>
<p>비공개 artifact는 “존재한다”까지만 쓴다. 필드/schema/content 주장은 public docs, source/bundle evidence, sanitized fixture, synthetic runtime trace가 있을 때만 쓴다.</p>

<h2>Reading Rule For Existing Docs</h2>
<p>When a <code>00</code>~<code>14</code> page says “없음” or “지원하지 않음”, interpret it as “installed help에서 노출되지 않음” unless this <code>15_reverse-engineering</code> axis confirms absence from bundle/binary evidence too.</p>
<p>When a page states runtime semantics from config/cache observation, this axis upgrades or downgrades the claim:</p>
<ul>
<li><code>bundle-key</code> or <code>binary-string</code> confirms a module exists.</li>
<li><code>runtime-trace</code> is still required for exact precedence, scheduling, isolation, merge, and permission behavior.</li>
</ul>

<h2>000/00_grand_synthesis.md (발췌)</h2>
<h1>GRAND SYNTHESIS — 5개 코딩 에이전트 × 13개 차원 최종 종합 분석</h1>
<p>이 문서는 Codex, Aider, Gemini CLI, OpenCode, Claude Code를 13개 아키텍처 차원에서 동시에 비교한 캡스톤 문서다.
개별 비교 문서의 결론을 단순 재배열하지 않고, 서로 다른 설계 철학이 어떤 제품 전략으로 수렴하는지까지 읽어내는 것을 목표로 한다.</p>
<pre><code class="language-mermaid">graph TD
    A[5개 에이전트 개요] --> B[13개 차원 비교]
    B --> C[공통 패턴 추출]
    B --> D[핵심 차별점 추출]
    C --> E[기술 선택 시사점]
    D --> E
    E --> F[미래 전망과 설계 교훈]
</code></pre>
<h2>1. 개요</h2>
<h3>이 문서의 목적</h3>
<p>이 문서의 목적은 5개 에이전트를 한 번에 조망할 수 있는 상위 레퍼런스를 만드는 것이다.
개별 문서는 특정 축의 우열을 설명하지만, 실제 제품 선택은 언제나 여러 축의 동시 판단을 요구한다.
따라서 여기서는 TUI, prompt, tool, skill, subagent, app-server, sandbox, config, MCP, memory, plugin, guardian, 그리고 잔여 교차 관심사를 하나의 프레임으로 다시 묶는다.</p>
<ul>
<li>근거: [[00_co_overview]], [[00_ai_overview]], [[00_ge_overview]], [[00_oc_overview]], [[00_cc_overview]]</li>
</ul>
<h3>분석 범위</h3>
<p>범위는 5개 에이전트와 13개 차원이다.
에이전트는 Codex, Aider, Gemini CLI, OpenCode, Claude Code다.
차원은 TUI, Prompt/Context, Tool Runtime, Skill, Subagents, App-Server Surface, Sandbox, Config, MCP, Memory, Plugin, Guardian, 잔여 교차 관심사(Git/VCS, 모델 라우팅, 에러 처리, 텔레메트리, IDE 통합, 패키징, 테스트, 인증, 멀티모달, 이벤트 시스템, 피처 플래그, 국제화)다.
App-Server 축은 비교 문서 자체가 Codex·Gemini CLI·OpenCode 중심으로 작성되어 있으므로 Aider와 Claude Code는 “의도적 부재”까지 함께 해석한다.</p>
<ul>
<li>근거: [[001_tui-design/00_tui]], [[002_prompt-context/00_prompt]], [[003_tool-runtime/00_tool]], [[004_skill-system/00_skill]], [[005_subagents-collab/00_subagent]], [[006_app-server-client-surfaces/00_surface]], [[007_sandbox-exec-policy/00_sandbox]], [[008_config-system/00_config]], [[009_mcp-orchestration/00_mcp]], [[010_memory-pipeline/00_memory]], [[011_plugin-system/00_plugin]], [[012_guardian-approval/00_guardian]], [[013_etc/00_etc]]</li>
</ul>
<h3>분석 방법론</h3>
<p>첫째, 각 에이전트 개요 문서에서 기술 스택, 패키지 구조, 핵심 철학을 추출했다.
둘째, 13개 비교 문서에서 축별 우위와 결손, 스카우팅 점수, 디자인 패턴을 수집했다.
셋째, 같은 에이전트가 여러 축에서 반복적으로 보이는 패턴을 묶어 장기 전략으로 재해석했다.
넷째, 단일 승자를 찾기보다 “어떤 상황에서 어떤 설계가 더 설득력 있는가”를 기준으로 실무 추천안을 도출했다.</p>
<ul>
<li>근거: [[00_co_overview]], [[00_ai_overview]], [[00_ge_overview]], [[00_oc_overview]], [[00_cc_overview]], [[001_tui-design/00_tui]], [[012_guardian-approval/00_guardian]]</li>
</ul>
<h3>이 문서를 읽는 방법</h3>
<p>제품 선택이 목적이면 3장, 7장, 8장을 먼저 보는 것이 좋다.
포크나 재구현이 목적이면 2장, 5장, 6장, 9장을 먼저 보는 것이 좋다.
보안 검토가 목적이면 3장, 4장, 8장, 9장을 함께 읽는 편이 낫다.
마지막 부록은 문서 인덱스 역할을 하므로 세부 원문으로 돌아갈 때 사용하면 된다.</p>
<ul>
<li>근거: [[007_sandbox-exec-policy/00_sandbox]], [[009_mcp-orchestration/00_mcp]], [[011_plugin-system/00_plugin]], [[012_guardian-approval/00_guardian]]</li>

<h3>Codex</h3>
<ul>
<li>정체성: 엔진을 층으로 분리하고, prompt·tool·skill·subagent·MCP를 제어면(control plane)으로 다룬다.</li>
<li>기술 스택: Rust + TypeScript + React/Ink + app-server protocol</li>
<li>핵심 차별점: 가장 분해 가능한 core engine, 가장 강한 terminal-native orchestration, 가장 균형 잡힌 sandbox/MCP 결합.</li>
<li>실무에서 강한 상황: 보안, 오케스트레이션, 포크 가능한 core engine이 중요한 팀</li>
<li>재구현 관점 한 줄 평: requirements 제약 채널과 prompt fragment provenance를 분리한 구조.</li>
<li>근거: [[00_co_overview]], [[001_tui-design/00_tui]], [[002_prompt-context/00_prompt]], [[003_tool-runtime/00_tool]], [[005_subagents-collab/00_subagent]], [[007_sandbox-exec-policy/00_sandbox]], [[009_mcp-orchestration/00_mcp]]</li>
</ul>

<li>기술 스택: Python + prompt_toolkit + rich + tree-sitter + Git</li>
